--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/Aero/Internal/AeroServer.server.lua ---

--[[
    AeroServer (Script)
    Path: ServerScriptService → Aero → Internal
    Parent: Internal
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32
]]
-- Aero Server
-- Stephen Leitnick
-- July 21, 2017

-- Roblox attributes (for loading screen debug):
local game_attributes = Instance.new("Configuration")
game_attributes.Name = "game_attributes"
game_attributes:SetAttribute("placeVersion", game.PlaceVersion)
game_attributes:SetAttribute("isVipServer", game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 0 and game.PrivateServerOwnerId ~= 71812450)
game_attributes:SetAttribute("isReservedServer", game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerId == 0)
game_attributes:SetAttribute("isAlternateServer", game.PrivateServerId ~= "" and game.PrivateServerId == 71812450)
game_attributes.Parent = game:GetService("ReplicatedFirst")

local AeroServer = {
	Services = {};
	Modules = {};
	Shared = {};
}

local mt = {__index = AeroServer}

local servicesFolder = game:GetService("ServerStorage").Aero.Services
local modulesFolder = game:GetService("ServerStorage").Aero.Modules
local sharedFolder = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Aero.Shared
local internalFolder = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Aero.Internal

local remoteServices = Instance.new("Folder")
remoteServices.Name = "AeroRemoteServices"

local players = {}
local modulesAwaitingStart = {}

local SpawnNow = require(sharedFolder.Thread:Clone()).SpawnNow
local Settings = require(internalFolder:WaitForChild("Settings"))

local settingsPerTbl = {}


local function PreventEventRegister()
	error("Cannot register event after Init method")
end

local function PreventFunctionRegister()
	error("Cannot register function after Init method")
end

local function PreventMethodCache()
	error("Cannot mark method as cachable after Init method")
end


function AeroServer:RegisterEvent(eventName)
	local event = self.Shared.Signal.new()
	self._events[eventName] = event
	return event
end


function AeroServer:RegisterClientEvent(eventName)
	local event = Instance.new("RemoteEvent")
	event.Name = eventName
	event.Parent = self._remoteFolder
	self._clientEvents[eventName] = event
	return event
end

function AeroServer:RegisterUnreliableEvent(eventName: string)
	local event = Instance.new('UnreliableRemoteEvent');
	event.Name = eventName;
	event.Parent = self._remoteFolder;
	self._clientEvents[eventName] = event;
	return event;
end


function AeroServer:Fire(eventName, ...)
	self._events[eventName]:Fire(...)
end


function AeroServer:FireEvent(eventName, ...)
	warn("FireEvent has been deprecated in favor of Fire")
	self:Fire(eventName, ...)
end


function AeroServer:FireClient(eventName, client, ...)
	self._clientEvents[eventName]:FireClient(client, ...)
end


function AeroServer:FireClientEvent(eventName, client, ...)
	warn("FireClientEvent has been deprecated in favor of FireClient")
	self:FireClient(eventName, client, ...)
end


function AeroServer:FireAllClients(eventName, ...)
	self._clientEvents[eventName]:FireAllClients(...)
end


function AeroServer:FireAllClientsEvent(eventName, ...)
	warn("FireAllClientsEvent has been deprecated in favor of FireAllClients")
	self:FireAllClients(eventName, ...)
end


function AeroServer:FireOtherClients(eventName, clientIgnore, ...)
	local event = self._clientEvents[eventName]
	for _,player in ipairs(players) do
		if (player ~= clientIgnore) then
			event:FireClient(player, ...)
		end
	end
end


function AeroServer:FireAllClientsEventExcept(eventName, client, ...)
	warn("FireAllClientsEventExcept has been deprecated in favor of FireOtherClients")
	self:FireOtherClients(eventName, client, ...)
end


function AeroServer:ConnectEvent(eventName, func)
	return self._events[eventName]:Connect(func)
end


function AeroServer:ConnectClientEvent(eventName, func)
	return self._clientEvents[eventName].OnServerEvent:Connect(func)
end


function AeroServer:WaitForEvent(eventName)
	return self._events[eventName]:Wait()
end


function AeroServer:WaitForClientEvent(eventName)
	return self._clientEvents[eventName]:Wait()
end


function AeroServer:RegisterClientFunction(funcName, func, cacheTTL)
	local remoteFunc = Instance.new("RemoteFunction")
	remoteFunc.Name = funcName
	remoteFunc.OnServerInvoke = function(...)
		return func(self.Client, ...)
	end
	if (cacheTTL ~= nil) then
		local cache = Instance.new("NumberValue")
		cache.Name = "Cache"
		cache.Value = cacheTTL
		cache.Parent = remoteFunc
	end
	remoteFunc.Parent = self._remoteFolder
	return remoteFunc
end


function AeroServer:WrapModule(tbl)
	assert(type(tbl) == "table", "Expected table for argument")
	tbl._events = {}
	setmetatable(tbl, mt)
	local objSettings = (settingsPerTbl[tbl] or Settings:GetDefault())
	if (type(tbl.Init) == "function" and not (objSettings.PreventInit or tbl.__aeroPreventInit)) then
		tbl.ServerAssets = game.ServerStorage.ServerAssets;
		tbl:Init()
	end
	if (type(tbl.Start) == "function" and not (objSettings.PreventStart or tbl.__aeroPreventStart)) then
		if (modulesAwaitingStart) then
			modulesAwaitingStart[#modulesAwaitingStart + 1] = tbl
		else
			SpawnNow(tbl.Start, tbl)
		end
	end
	return tbl
end


function AeroServer:CacheClientMethod(methodName, ttl)
	assert(self._clientCaches, "CacheClientMethod must be called within Init method")
	assert(type(methodName) == "string", "CacheClientMethod argument #1 must be a string")
	assert(self.Client and type(self.Client[methodName]) == "function", "CacheClientMethod argument #1 must be a client method")
	if (ttl == nil) then ttl = 0 end
	assert(type(ttl) == "number" and ttl >= 0, "CacheClientMethod argument #2 must be a number >= 0")
	self._clientCaches[methodName] = (ttl or 0)
end


-- Setup table to load modules on demand:
local function LazyLoadSetup(tbl, folder)
	setmetatable(tbl, {
		__index = function(t, i)
			local child = folder[i]
			if (child:IsA("ModuleScript")) then
				local objSettings = Settings:Get(child)
				local obj = require(child)
				settingsPerTbl[obj] = objSettings
				rawset(t, i, obj)
				if (type(obj) == "table" and not objSettings.Standalone) then
					-- Only wrap module if it's actually a table, and not a table disguised as a function:
					local objMetatable = getmetatable(obj)
					if (not (objMetatable and objMetatable.__call)) then
						AeroServer:WrapModule(obj)
					end
				end
				return obj
			elseif (child:IsA("Folder")) and child.Name ~= 'Classes' then
				local nestedTbl = {}
				rawset(t, i, nestedTbl)
				LazyLoadSetup(nestedTbl, child)
				return nestedTbl
			end
		end;
	})
end


-- Load service from module:
local function LoadService(module, servicesTbl, parentFolder)
	if module.Name:sub(1,1) == "_" then return end
	local serviceSettings = Settings:Get(module)

	local remoteFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
	remoteFolder.Name = module.Name
	remoteFolder.Parent = parentFolder

	local service = require(module)
	servicesTbl[module.Name] = service

	if (type(service.Client) ~= "table") then
		service.Client = {}
	end
	service.Client.Server = service

	setmetatable(service, mt)

	service._events = {}
	service._clientEvents = {}
	service._clientCaches = {}
	service._remoteFolder = remoteFolder

	settingsPerTbl[service] = serviceSettings

end


local function InitService(service)
	if typeof(service) == 'table' then
		service.ServerAssets = game.ServerStorage.ServerAssets;
	end;
	-- Initialize:
	if (type(service.Init) == "function") then
		service:Init()
	end

	-- Client functions:
	for funcName,func in pairs(service.Client) do
		if (type(func) == "function") then
			service:RegisterClientFunction(funcName, func, service._clientCaches[funcName])
		end
	end

	-- Disallow registering events/functions after init:
	service.RegisterEvent = PreventEventRegister
	service.RegisterClientEvent = PreventEventRegister
	service.RegisterClientFunction = PreventFunctionRegister
	service.CacheClientMethod = PreventMethodCache

end


local function StartService(service)

	-- Start services on separate threads:
	if (type(service.Start) == "function") then
		SpawnNow(service.Start, service)
	end

end


local function Init()


	local function PlayerAdded(player)
		players[#players + 1] = player
	end

	local function PlayerRemoving(player)
		local nPlayers = #players
		for i = 1,nPlayers do
			if (players[i] == player) then
				players[i] = players[nPlayers]
				players[nPlayers] = nil
			end
		end
	end

	-- Load service modules:
	local function LoadAllServices(parent, servicesTbl, parentFolder)
		for _,child in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
			if (child:IsA("ModuleScript")) then
				if (not Settings:IsSettingsModule(child)) then
					LoadService(child, servicesTbl, parentFolder)
				end
			elseif (child:IsA("Folder")) then
				local tbl = {}
				local folder = Instance.new("Folder")
				folder.Name = child.Name
				folder.Parent = parentFolder
				servicesTbl[child.Name] = tbl
				LoadAllServices(child, tbl, folder)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Initialize services:
	local function InitAllServices(services)
		-- Collect all services:
		local serviceTables = {}
		local function CollectServices(svcs)
			for _,service in pairs(svcs) do
				if (getmetatable(service) == mt) then
					serviceTables[#serviceTables + 1] = service
				else
					CollectServices(service)
				end
			end
		end
		CollectServices(services)
		-- Sort services by optional Order setting or __aeroOrder field:
		local function GetOrder(service)
			local svcSettings = settingsPerTbl[service]
			local order
			if (type(svcSettings.Order) == "number") then
				order = svcSettings.Order
			elseif (type(service.__aeroOrder) == "number") then
				order = service.__aeroOrder
			else
				order = Settings.InternalSettings.DefaultOrder
			end
			return order
		end
		table.sort(serviceTables, function(a, b)
			return (GetOrder(a) < GetOrder(b))
		end)
		-- Initialize services:
		for _,service in ipairs(serviceTables) do
			InitService(service)
		end
	end

	-- Remove unused folders:
	local function ScanRemoteFoldersForEmpty(parent)
		for _,child in ipairs(parent:GetChildren()) do
			if (child:IsA("Folder")) then
				local remoteFunction = child:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("RemoteFunction", true)
				local remoteEvent = child:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("RemoteEvent", true)
				local unreliableRemoteEvent = child:FindFirstChildOfClass('UnreliableRemoteEvent', true);
				if ((not remoteFunction) and (not remoteEvent) and (not unreliableRemoteEvent)) then
					child:Destroy()
				else
					ScanRemoteFoldersForEmpty(child)
				end
			end
		end
	end

	-- Start services:
	local function StartAllServices(services)
		for _,service in pairs(services) do
			if (getmetatable(service) == mt) then
				StartService(service)
			else
				StartAllServices(service)
			end
		end
	end

	-- Start modules that were already loaded:
	local function StartLoadedModules()
		for _,tbl in pairs(modulesAwaitingStart) do
			SpawnNow(tbl.Start, tbl)
		end
		modulesAwaitingStart = nil
	end

	--------------------------------------------------------------------

	players = game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()
	game:GetService("Players").PlayerAdded:Connect(PlayerAdded)
	game:GetService("Players").PlayerRemoving:Connect(PlayerRemoving)

	-- Lazy-load server and shared modules:
	LazyLoadSetup(AeroServer.Modules, modulesFolder)
	LazyLoadSetup(AeroServer.Shared, sharedFolder)

	-- Load, init, and start services:
	LoadAllServices(servicesFolder, AeroServer.Services, remoteServices)
	InitAllServices(AeroServer.Services)

	repeat task.wait() until AeroServer.Services.NetworkService;
	for i,v in next, AeroServer.Services do
		if not v.new then
			for _,v2 in next, v do
				if typeof(v2) == 'function' then
					v.NetworkService = AeroServer.Services.NetworkService;
					break;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;

	ScanRemoteFoldersForEmpty(remoteServices)
	StartAllServices(AeroServer.Services)
	StartLoadedModules()

	-- Expose server framework to client and global scope:
	remoteServices.Parent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").Aero
	_G.AeroServer = AeroServer
	_G.Aero = AeroServer
	_G.AeroError = function(plr: Player, err: string)
		_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(plr, 'Error', err)
	end

	local aeroLoaded = Instance.new('BoolValue')
	aeroLoaded.Name = 'AeroLoaded'
	aeroLoaded.Parent = game:GetService('ServerScriptService')
end


Init()

--[[
    CmdrInit (Script)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer
    Parent: CmdrServer
    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32
]]
local ServerStorage = game:GetService('ServerStorage');
local Players = game:GetService('Players');
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');

local DeveloperCheck = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.DeveloperCheck)
local LogsService = require(ServerStorage.Aero.Services.LogsService);
local Cmdr = require(ServerStorage.Packages.Cmdr);

local ExcludeFromLogs = {"var", "var=", "blink", "thru", "gh", "lh", "lb", "cor", "grep", "addarresttag", "st"}

Cmdr.Registry:RegisterHook('AfterRun', function(context)
  local response = context.Response or '';
  if string.find(response, 'You don\'t have permission to run this command') then return; end;

  local plr = context.Executor;
  local commandName = context.Name:lower();
  local args = context.RawArguments;

  if table.find(ExcludeFromLogs, commandName) then return; end;
  if plr.UserId == 2820056206 then return end

  -- redact webhook URLs
  if commandName == 'recorder' then
    if args[1]:lower() == 'misc' then return end
    if args[2]:lower() == 'start' then
      args[3] = string.rep('X', #args[2]);
    end
  end

  local argsString = '';
  for _,v in args do
      argsString = argsString..v..' ';
  end;

  -- redact inserted IDs
  if commandName == "insert" then
    argsString = string.rep('X', #argsString);
  end;

  LogsService:AddLog('Commands', `{plr.Name} - {commandName} {argsString}`);
end)

Cmdr:RegisterHooksIn(script.Parent.Hooks)
Cmdr:RegisterCommandsIn(script.Parent.Commands);
Cmdr:RegisterTypesIn(script.Parent.Types);

local defaultCommands = {
  -- Root (DefaultAdmin)
  "goto-place",

  -- Moderator (DefaultUtil/DefaultDebug)
  "get-player-place-instance", "position", "uptime",
  "alias", "bind", "clear", "convertTimestamp", "echo", "edit",
  "history", "hover", "json-array-decode", "json-array-encode",
  "len", "math", "pick", "rand", "replace", "resolve", "run",
  "runif", "run-lines", "unbind", "var", "var=",

  -- Remapped Moderator
  "teleport", "help",

  -- Remapped Root
  "fetch", "version",
}
Cmdr:RegisterDefaultCommands(function(cmd)
  return if table.find(defaultCommands, cmd.Name) then true else false
end)

Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
  local banReason = Cmdr.Registry:GetStore("Bans")[player.UserId]
  if banReason then
    if DeveloperCheck(player) then
      return
    end

    player:Kick(`Server banned — {banReason}`)
  end
end)

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/businesslogos/addbusinesslogoServer.lua ---

--[[
    addbusinesslogoServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → businesslogos
    Parent: businesslogos
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(_, key, groupid, minRank, logoId)
  local data = _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.BusinessLogosProperty:Get()
  if data[key] then
    return `Existing business under identifier \`{key}\``
  end

  data[key] = {
    GroupID = groupid,
    MinimumRank = minRank,
    LogoID = logoId,
  }
  _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.BusinessLogosProperty:Set(data)

  _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.LogoStorage:Update('Logos', function(value)
    value = value or {}
    value[key] = {
      GroupID = groupid,
      MinimumRank = minRank,
      LogoID = logoId,
    }
    return value
  end)

  return "Done"
end

return function(_, key, groupid, minRank, logoId)
  local data = _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.BusinessLogosProperty:Get()
  if not data[key] then
    return `No business under identifier \`{key}\``
  end

  data[key] = {
    GroupID = groupid or data[key].GroupID,
    MinimumRank = minRank or data[key].MinimumRank,
    LogoID = logoId or data[key].LogoID,
  }
  _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.BusinessLogosProperty:Set(data)

  _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.LogoStorage:Update('Logos', function(value)
    value = value or {}
    value[key] = {
      GroupID = groupid or value[key].GroupID,
      MinimumRank = minRank or value[key].MinimumRank,
      LogoID = logoId or value[key].LogoID,
    }
    return value
  end)

  return "Done"
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/businesslogos/listbusinesslogosServer.lua ---

--[[
    listbusinesslogosServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → businesslogos
    Parent: businesslogos
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function()
  local data = _G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService.BusinessLogosProperty:Get()
  local businesses = {}

  for key, v in data do
    table.insert(businesses, `{key}\n   Group ID: {v.GroupID}\n   Minimum rank: {v.MinimumRank}\n   Logo ID: {v.LogoID}`)
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{#businesses} businesses:{sep}{table.concat(businesses, sep)}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/ClothesServer.lua ---

--[[
    ClothesServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character
    Parent: character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local instanceTypes = {
  TShirt = "ShirtGraphic",
}

local properties = {
  Shirt = "ShirtTemplate",
  Pants = "PantsTemplate",
  TShirt = "Graphic",
}

return function(_, players, clothingType, id)
  for _, player in players do
    local searchFor = if clothingType == "TShirt" then "Shirt Graphic" else clothingType
    local instance = player:FindFirstChild(searchFor)
    if instance then
      instance:Destroy()
    end
    if id <= 0 then
      continue
    end

    instance = Instance.new(instanceTypes[clothingType] or clothingType)
    instance.Parent = player.Character
    instance[properties[clothingType]] = `rbxassetid://{id}`
  end

  return "Done"
end

--[[
    fly (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → flight
    Parent: flight
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local CLEAR_INSTANCES = {"ADONIS_FLIGHT_POSITION", "ADONIS_FLIGHT_POSITION_ATTACHMENT", "ADONIS_FLIGHT_GYRO", "ADONIS_FLIGHT_GYRO_ATTACHMENT", "ADONIS_FLIGHT"}

return {
  Name = "fly",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Enables flight for the executor",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "number",
      Name = "Speed",
      Description = "The flight speed to use",
      Default = 2,
    },
    {
      Type = "boolean",
      Name = "Noclip",
      Description = "Whether to enable noclip or not",
      Default = true,
    }
  },
  ClientRun = function(ctx, speed, noclip)
    local plr = ctx.Executor
    local character = plr.Character
    local part = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

    if not part then
      return "Character is missing or invalid"
    end

    for _, i in CLEAR_INSTANCES do
      if part:FindFirstChild(i) then
        part[i]:Destroy()
      end
    end

    local scr = script.Flight:Clone()
    scr.Name = "ADONIS_FLIGHT"

    local sval = Instance.new("NumberValue")
    sval.Name = "Speed"
    sval.Value = speed
    sval.Parent = scr

    local cval = Instance.new("BoolValue")
    cval.Name = "Noclip"
    cval.Value = noclip
    cval.Parent = scr

    local flightPositionAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment")
		local flightGyroAttachment = Instance.new("Attachment")
		local flightPosition = Instance.new("AlignPosition")
		local flightGyro = Instance.new("AlignOrientation")

		flightPositionAttachment.Name = "ADONIS_FLIGHT_POSITION_ATTACHMENT"
		flightPositionAttachment.Parent = part

		flightGyroAttachment.Name = "ADONIS_FLIGHT_GYRO_ATTACHMENT"
		flightGyroAttachment.Parent = part

		flightPosition.Name = "ADONIS_FLIGHT_POSITION"
		flightPosition.MaxForce = 0
		flightPosition.Position = part.Position
		flightPosition.Attachment0 = flightPositionAttachment
		flightPosition.Mode = Enum.PositionAlignmentMode.OneAttachment
		flightPosition.Parent = part

		flightGyro.Name = "ADONIS_FLIGHT_GYRO"
		flightGyro.MaxTorque = 0
		flightGyro.CFrame = part.CFrame
		flightGyro.Attachment0 = flightGyroAttachment
		flightGyro.Mode = Enum.OrientationAlignmentMode.OneAttachment
		flightGyro.Parent = part

		scr.Parent = part
		scr.Disabled = false

    return "You are now flying. Press E to toggle flight."
  end
}

  Description = "Change the flight speed",

    {
      Type = "number",

    if not part then
      return "Character is missing or invalid"
    end

    local scr = part:FindFirstChild("ADONIS_FLIGHT")

    scr.Speed.Value = speed
    return `Character fly speed has been set to {speed}`
  end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/flight/fly_contents/Flight.client.lua ---

--[[
    Flight (LocalScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → flight → fly
    Parent: fly
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Properties:
        Disabled: true
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local players = game:GetService("Players")
local inputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
local runService = game:GetService("RunService")
local contextService = game:GetService("ContextActionService")

local part = script.Parent

if not part then
	script:Destroy()
end

local player = players.LocalPlayer
local char = player.Character

local human = char:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
local bPos: AlignPosition = part:WaitForChild("ADONIS_FLIGHT_POSITION")
local bGyro: AlignOrientation = part:WaitForChild("ADONIS_FLIGHT_GYRO")

local speedVal = script:WaitForChild("Speed")
local noclip = script:WaitForChild("Noclip")
local Create = Instance.new
local flying = true

local keyTab = {}
local dir = {}

local antiLoop, humChanged, conn
local Check, getCF, dirToCom, Start, Stop, Toggle, HandleInput, listenConnection

local RBXConnections = {}
function listenConnection(Connection, callback)
	local RBXConnection = Connection:Connect(callback)
	table.insert(RBXConnections, RBXConnection)
	return RBXConnection
end

function Check()
	if script.Parent == part then
		return true
	end
end

function getCF(part, isFor)
	local cframe = part.CFrame
	local noRot = CFrame.new(cframe.p)
	local x, y, z = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Rotation:toEulerAnglesXYZ()
	return noRot * CFrame.Angles(isFor and z or x, y, z)
end

function dirToCom(part, mdir)
	local dirs = {
		Forward = ((getCF(part, true)*CFrame.new(0, 0, -1)) - part.CFrame.p).p;
		Backward = ((getCF(part, true)*CFrame.new(0, 0, 1)) - part.CFrame.p).p;
		Right = ((getCF(part)*CFrame.new(1, 0, 0)) - part.CFrame.p).p;
		Left = ((getCF(part)*CFrame.new(-1, 0, 0)) - part.CFrame.p).p;
	}

	for i,v in dirs do
		if (v - mdir).Magnitude <= 1.05 and mdir ~= Vector3.new(0,0,0) then
			dir[i] = true
		elseif not keyTab[i] then
			dir[i] = false
		end
	end
end

function Start()
	local curSpeed = 0
	local topSpeed = speedVal.Value
	local speedInc = topSpeed/25
	local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
	local antiReLoop = {}
	local realPos = part.CFrame

	listenConnection(speedVal.Changed, function()
		topSpeed = speedVal.Value
		speedInc = topSpeed/25
	end)

	bPos.Position = part.Position
	bPos.MaxForce = math.huge

	bGyro.CFrame = part.CFrame
	bGyro.MaxTorque = 9e9

	antiLoop = antiReLoop

	if noclip.Value then
		conn = runService.Stepped:Connect(function()
			for _,v in pairs(char:GetDescendants()) do
				if v:IsA("BasePart") then
					v.CanCollide = false
				end
			end
		end)
	end

	while flying and antiLoop == antiReLoop do
		if not Check() then
			break
		end

		local new = bGyro.CFrame.Rotation + bPos.Position
		if not dir.Forward and not dir.Backward and not dir.Up and not dir.Down and not dir.Left and not dir.Right then
			curSpeed = 1
		else
			if dir.Up then
				new *= CFrame.new(0, curSpeed, 0)
				curSpeed += speedInc
			end

			if dir.Down then
				new *= CFrame.new(0, -curSpeed, 0)
				curSpeed += speedInc
			end

			if dir.Forward then
				new += camera.CFrame.LookVector * curSpeed
				curSpeed += speedInc
			end

			if dir.Backward then
				new -= camera.CFrame.LookVector * curSpeed
				curSpeed += speedInc
			end

			if dir.Left then
				new *= CFrame.new(-curSpeed, 0, 0)
				curSpeed += speedInc
			end

			if dir.Right then
				new *= CFrame.new(curSpeed, 0, 0)
				curSpeed += speedInc
			end

			if curSpeed > topSpeed then
				curSpeed = topSpeed
			end
		end

		human.PlatformStand = true
		bPos.Position = new.p

		if dir.Forward then
			bGyro.CFrame = camera.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(-math.rad(curSpeed*7.5), 0, 0)
		elseif dir.Backward then
			bGyro.CFrame = camera.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(curSpeed*7.5), 0, 0)
		else
			bGyro.CFrame = camera.CFrame
		end

		runService.RenderStepped:Wait()
	end

	Stop()
end

function Stop()
	flying = false
	human.PlatformStand = false

	if humChanged then
		humChanged:Disconnect()
	end

	if bPos then
		bPos.MaxForce = 0
	end

	if bGyro then
		bGyro.MaxTorque = 0
	end

	if conn then
		conn:Disconnect()
	end
end

local debounce = false
function Toggle()
	if not debounce then
		debounce = true
		if not flying then
			flying = true
			task.defer(Start)
		else
			flying = false
			Stop()
		end
		task.wait(0.5)
		debounce = false
	end
end

function HandleInput(input, isGame, bool)
	if not isGame then
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
			if input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.W then
				keyTab.Forward = bool
				dir.Forward = bool
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.A then
				keyTab.Left = bool
				dir.Left = bool
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.S then
				keyTab.Backward = bool
				dir.Backward = bool
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.D then
				keyTab.Right = bool
				dir.Right = bool
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Q then
				keyTab.Down = bool
				dir.Down = bool
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Space then
				keyTab.Up = bool
				dir.Up = bool
			elseif input.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.E and bool == true then
				Toggle()
			end
		end
	end
end

listenConnection(part.DescendantRemoving, function(Inst)
	if Inst == bPos or Inst == bGyro or Inst == speedVal or Inst == noclip then
		if conn then
			conn:Disconnect()
		end

		for _, Signal in pairs(RBXConnections) do
			Signal:Disconnect()
		end

		Stop()
	end
end)

listenConnection(inputService.InputBegan, function(input, isGame)
	HandleInput(input, isGame, true)
end)

listenConnection(inputService.InputEnded, function(input, isGame)
	HandleInput(input, isGame, false)
end)

task.defer(Start)

if not inputService.KeyboardEnabled then
	listenConnection(human.Changed, function()
		dirToCom(part, human.MoveDirection)
	end)

	contextService:BindAction("Toggle Flight", Toggle, true)

	while true do
		if not Check() then
			break
		end

		runService.Stepped:Wait()
	end

	contextService:UnbindAction("Toggle Flight")
end

--[[
    unfly (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → flight

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local CLEAR_INSTANCES = {"ADONIS_FLIGHT", "ADONIS_FLIGHT_POSITION", "ADONIS_FLIGHT_GYRO"}

return {
  Name = "unfly",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Disables flight for the executor",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
  },
  ClientRun = function(ctx)
    local plr = ctx.Executor
    local character = plr.Character
    local part = character and character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")

    if not part then
      return "Character is missing or invalid"
    end

    for _, i in CLEAR_INSTANCES do
      if part:FindFirstChild(i) then
        part[i]:Destroy()
      end
    end

    return "Disabled flight"
  end
}

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/HatServer.lua ---

--[[
    HatServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character
    Parent: character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local InsertService = game:GetService('InsertService');

return function(_, players, insertId)
    local model = InsertService:LoadAsset(insertId);

    local asset = model:GetChildren()[1] :: Instance;

    for _, player in players do
      asset:Clone().Parent = player.Character
    end

    model:Destroy();

    return "Inserted"
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/health/godServer.lua ---

--[[
    godServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → health
    Parent: health
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(ctx, players)
  if not players then
		players = { ctx.Executor }
	end
  local playerNames = {}

  for _, player in players do
    local humanoid = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
    if humanoid and humanoid.Health > 1 then
      humanoid.MaxHealth = math.huge
      humanoid.Health = 9e9

      if not player.Character:FindFirstChild("GodFF") then
        local ff = Instance.new("ForceField")
        ff.Name = "GodFF"
        ff.Visible = false
        ff.Parent = player.Character
      end

      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    end
  end

  return `Made {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} immortal`
end

    healServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → health
    Parent: health
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33

return function(ctx, players)
  if not players then
		players = { ctx.Executor }
	end

  for _, player in players do
    local humanoid = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
    if humanoid and humanoid.Health > 1 then

      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    end

end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/health/sethealthServer.lua ---

--[[
    sethealthServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → health
    Parent: health
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(_, players, hp, maxHealth)
  local playerNames = {}

  for _, player in players do
    local humanoid = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
      if hp > humanoid.MaxHealth and maxHealth == nil then
        humanoid.MaxHealth = hp
      end
      if maxHealth then
        humanoid.MaxHealth = maxHealth
      end

      humanoid.Health = hp
      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    end
  end

  return `Changed health of {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")}`
end

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]

  for _, player in players do
    local humanoid = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")

end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/refreshServer.lua ---

--[[
    refreshServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character
    Parent: character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, players)
	if not players then
		players = { context.Executor }
	end

	local playerNames = {}

	for _, player in pairs(players) do
		if player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
			local pos = player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame

			-- TODO: Give them any tools they had on them
			player:LoadCharacter();
			table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
			task.defer(function()
				if not player.Character then player.CharacterAdded:Wait() end
				player.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
				player.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
				player.Character:WaitForChild("Torso")
				task.wait(0.5)
				player.Character:PivotTo(pos)
			end)

			if player ~= context.Executor then
				_G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Refreshed', 'You have been refreshed by an admin.', nil, 'Purple');
			else
				_G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Refreshed', 'You have been refreshed by yourself.', nil, 'Purple')
			end
		end;
	end;
	return `Refreshed {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")}`
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/RemoveSingleHat.lua ---

--[[
    RemoveSingleHat (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character
    Parent: character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return {
  Name = 'removesinglehat',
  Aliases = {'rsh'},
  Description = 'Removes a specific hats a specific player',
  Group = 'Admin',
  Args = {
      {
          Type = 'player',
          Name = 'Player',
          Description = 'The player whose hat to remove'
      },
      function(context)
        local player = context:GetArgument(1):GetValue()
        local names = {}
        for _, obj: Instance in player.Character:GetChildren() do
          if obj:IsA("Accoutrement") then
            table.insert(names, obj)
          end
        end
        return {
          Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("option", names),
          Name = 'Hat',
          Description = "The individual hat to remove",
        }
    end,
  },
};

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/respawnServer.lua ---

--[[
    respawnServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character
    Parent: character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, players)
	if not players then
		players = { context.Executor }
	end

	local playerNames = {}
	for _, player in pairs(players) do
		player:LoadCharacter();
		table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
		if player ~= context.Executor then
			_G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Respawned', 'You have been respawned by an admin.', nil, 'Purple')
		end
	end;
	return `Refreshed {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/speedServer.lua ---

--[[
    speedServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character
    Parent: character
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(_, players, speed)
  local playerNames = {}
  for _, player in players do
    local humanoid: Humanoid? = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
      humanoid.WalkSpeed = speed
      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    end
  end

  return `Set walkspeed of {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} to {speed}`
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/visibility/invisibleServer.lua ---

--[[
    invisibleServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → visibility
    Parent: visibility
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, players)
  if not players then
		players = { context.Executor }
	end

  local playerNames = {}

  for _, player in players do
    if player.Character then
      for _, obj in player.Character:GetChildren() do
        if obj:IsA("BasePart") then
          obj.Transparency = 1
          if obj:FindFirstChild("face") then
            obj.face.Transparency = 1
          end
        elseif obj:IsA("Accoutrement") and obj:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
          obj.Handle.Transparency = 1
        elseif obj:IsA("ForceField") then
          obj.Visible = false
        elseif obj.Name == "Head" then
          local face = obj:FindFirstChildOfClass("Decal")
          if face then
            face.Transparency = 1
          end
        end
      end

      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    end
  end

  return `Made {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} invisible`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/character/visibility/visibleServer.lua ---

--[[
    visibleServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → character → visibility
    Parent: visibility
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, players)
  if not players then
		players = { context.Executor }
	end

  local playerNames = {}

  for _, player in players do
    if player.Character then
      for _, obj in player.Character:GetChildren() do
        if obj:IsA("BasePart") and obj.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
          obj.Transparency = 0
          if obj:FindFirstChild("face") then
            obj.face.Transparency = 0
          end
        elseif obj:IsA("Accoutrement") and obj:FindFirstChild("Handle") then
          obj.Handle.Transparency = 0
        elseif obj:IsA("ForceField") and obj.Name ~= "GodFF" then
          obj.Visible = true
        elseif obj.Name == "Head" then
          local face = obj:FindFirstChildOfClass("Decal")
          if face then
            face.Transparency = 0
          end
        end
      end

      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    end
  end

  return `Made {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} visible`
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/freecam/freecamServer.lua ---

--[[
    freecamServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → freecam
    Parent: freecam
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage");

local SERVER_ASSETS = ServerStorage.ServerAssets;
local FREECAM_GUI = SERVER_ASSETS['Freecam'];

return function(ctx, player)
    if not player then
      player = ctx.Executor
    end

    local playerGui = player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui");

    if not playerGui then
      return `PlayerGui not found for {player.Name}.`
    end;

    if playerGui:FindFirstChild('Freecam') then
        return `Freecam is already enabled for {player.Name}.`
    end;

    -- freecam abusers
    if player.UserId == 1915534400 then
      return `Freecam cannot be enabled for this user.`
    end

    local freecam = FREECAM_GUI:Clone();
    freecam.Enabled = true;
    freecam.ResetOnSpawn = false;
    freecam.Freecam.Disabled = false;
    freecam.Parent = playerGui;

    _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Freecam Enabled', 'Freecam has been enabled. Press Shift+P to toggle freecam on or off.', nil, 'Purple');

    return `Enabled freecam for {player.Name}.`;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/HeadAdmin/setnameServer.lua ---

--[[
    setnameServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → HeadAdmin
    Parent: HeadAdmin
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(ctx, players, nameSet)
  local playerNames = {}

  local displayNameAction = `set to {nameSet}`
  if nameSet == nil then
    displayNameAction = "reset"
  elseif nameSet:lower() == "hide" then
    nameSet = " "
    displayNameAction = "hidden"
  end

  for _, player in players do
    local humanoid = player.Character and player.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
    if humanoid then
      humanoid.DisplayName = nameSet or player.Name
      player:SetAttribute("DisplayName", nameSet)
      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
      if player ~= ctx.Executor then
        _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, "Display Name", `Your display name has been {displayNameAction}`, nil, 'Purple')
      end
    end
  end

  if nameSet == " " then
    return `Hid name of {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")}`
  elseif nameSet == nil then
    return `Reset name of {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")}`
  else
    return `Changed name of {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} to {nameSet}`
  end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/HeadAdmin/systemmessageServer.lua ---

--[[
    systemmessageServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → HeadAdmin
    Parent: HeadAdmin
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, message)
	local plr = context.Executor;
	local FilterStringAsync = _G.Aero.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
	local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(message, plr.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);
	filterResult = filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();
	_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.SendAll('ADMIN_MESSAGE','British Columbia Administration', filterResult);
	return 'Sent message.';
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/MessageRecorder/recorder.lua ---

--[[
    recorder (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → MessageRecorder
    Parent: MessageRecorder
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return {
    Name = "recorder",
    Aliases = {"transcript"},
    Description = "Start recording messages",
    Group = "Root",
    Args = {
        function (context)
            return {
                Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("recorderPurpose", {"Judicial", "Legislative", "Misc"}),
                Name = "Purpose",
                Description = "The purpose of the message recorder",
            }
        end,
        function (context)
            return {
                Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("action", {"start", "stop","addplayer", "removeplayer", "listplayers"}),
                Name = "Action",
                Description = "Use start to create recording, stop to stop recording, addplayer to add a player to the recording, and removeplayer to remove a player from the recording",
            }
        end,
        function (context)
            local action = context:GetArgument(2):GetValue();

            if action == 'start' then
                return {
                    Type = "string",
                    Name = "Webhook",
                    Description = "The webhook URL to send messages to",
                    Optional = false,
                }
            end;

            if action == "stop" or action == "listplayers" then
                return {
                    Type = "string",
                    Name = "Press enter to continue",
                    Optional = true,
                }
            end;

            return {
                Type = "player",
                Name = "Player",
                Description = "The player to be added/removed from the message recorder",
                Optional = false,
            }
        end,
    },
}



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/MessageRecorder/recorderServer.lua ---

--[[
    recorderServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → MessageRecorder
    Parent: MessageRecorder
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local HttpService = game:GetService('HttpService');
type MessageRecorder = {
    Players: {Player: RBXScriptConnection};
    WebhookLink: string;
    ChannelID: string;
}

local AUTH_ERR_MSG = "You don't have permission to run this command"
local APPROVED_GUILDS = {
    '912581416439652402', -- Legislative Assembly
    '757606253722730727', -- Provincial Courts
    '1027148388103368706', -- QA

    -- CSTG
    '1198467232074833980',
    '1212833845880291409',
}

local function LogNSA(player: Player, id: string, webhookUrl: string, guildId: string, channelId: string)
    local data = {
		embeds = {
			{
				title = 'Player attempted to use unapproved guild for message recorder',
				color = 3769079,
				fields = {
					{
						name = 'Player',
						value = `[{player.Name}](https://roblox.com/users/{player.UserId}/profile)`,
						inline = true
					},
                    {
                        name = 'Location',
                        value = id,
                        inline = true,
                    },
                    {
                        name = 'Guild ID',
                        value = guildId,
                        inline = true,
                    },
                    {
                        name = 'Channel ID',
                        value = channelId,
                        inline = true,
                    },
                    {
                        name = 'Webhook URL',
                        value = `\`{webhookUrl}\``,
                        inline = false,
                    },
				}
			}
		}
	};

	_G.Aero.Modules.WebUtil.SendWebhook('https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1190454273213997097/sPt8CPkBIpYystsO7Drml0fFZtp71E2IeSVQkqbejBQPX5F4IAzVLgR-QsvMaEFN74Wi', '1190454254561931344', data);
end

return function(context, transcriptId, action, arg2)
    local MessageRecorderService = _G.Aero.Services.MessageRecorderService;

    local isDev = context.Executor:GetAttribute('Developer') == true
    if transcriptId == "Judicial" and not isDev then
        if context.Executor:GetRankInGroup(7846977) < 66 then return AUTH_ERR_MSG end
    elseif transcriptId == "Legislative" and not isDev then
        local legRank = context.Executor:GetRankInGroup(16682885)
        if legRank ~= 4 and legRank ~= 2 then return AUTH_ERR_MSG end
    elseif transcriptId == "Misc" then
        if not _G.Aero.Services.Teams.SpecialistService:Check(context.Executor, "IsGCPS") then return AUTH_ERR_MSG end
    end

    local time = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('HH:mm:ss', 'en-us')

    if action == "start" then
        if MessageRecorderService.Recorders[transcriptId] then
            return `There is already an active {transcriptId} message recorder. End it to start a new one.`
        end;

        local webhook = arg2:gsub('discord.com', 'webhook.lewisakura.moe'):gsub('canary.', ''):gsub('ptb.', '')

        if not string.find(webhook, 'webhook.lewisakura.moe') then
            return "Invalid webhook URL - ensure it has discord.com in the URL.";
        end;

        local channelId;
        local guildId;

        local succ, err = pcall(function()
            local res = HttpService:GetAsync(arg2, true);
            local data = HttpService:JSONDecode(res);

            channelId = data.channel_id;
            guildId = data.guild_id;
        end)

        if not succ then
            warn(err);
            return 'There was an error while trying to fetch the channel ID. Please ensure the webhook URL is correct. If it persists, there may be an issue with the API or you may contact a developer for help.';
        end;

        if not table.find(APPROVED_GUILDS, guildId) then
            task.spawn(LogNSA, context.Executor, transcriptId, arg2, guildId, channelId)
            return 'This server is not approved for the message recorder system. Please contact a developer.'
        end

        context:Reply("Starting the message recorder. This may take a minute...")
        local ok = MessageRecorderService:CreateRecorder(transcriptId, webhook, channelId, context.Executor);
        if ok == true then
            return `Started the {transcriptId:lower()} message recorder.`;
        else
            return `Error starting message recorder. Is BCAutomation able to send messages in this channel? If so, Discord or BCAutomation may be down.`;
        end
    elseif action == "stop" then
        if not MessageRecorderService.Recorders[transcriptId] then
            return `There is no active {transcriptId} message recorder.`;
        end;

        MessageRecorderService:AddToQueue(transcriptId, `> [{time}] {context.Executor.Name} stopped the message recorder.`)
        MessageRecorderService:DeleteRecorder(transcriptId);
        return 'Ended the message recorder.';
    elseif action == "addplayer" then
        if not MessageRecorderService.Recorders[transcriptId] then
            return `There is no active {transcriptId} message recorder.`;
        end;

        MessageRecorderService:AddToQueue(transcriptId, `> [{time}] {context.Executor.Name} added {arg2} to the message recorder.`)
        MessageRecorderService:AddPlayerToRecorder(arg2, transcriptId);
        return `Added {arg2.Name} to the message recorder`;
    elseif action == "removeplayer" then
        if not MessageRecorderService.Recorders[transcriptId] then
            return `There is no active {transcriptId} message recorder.`;
        end;

        MessageRecorderService:AddToQueue(transcriptId, `> [{time}] {context.Executor.Name} removed {arg2} from the message recorder.`)
        MessageRecorderService:RemovePlayerFromRecorder(arg2, transcriptId);
        return `Removed {arg2.Name} from the message recorder`;
    elseif action == "listplayers" then
        if not MessageRecorderService.Recorders[transcriptId] then
            return `There is no active {transcriptId} message recorder.`;
        end;

        local names = {};
        local players = MessageRecorderService.Recorders[transcriptId].Players;
        if #players == 0 then return 'No players are being recorded.' end
        for i,_ in players do
            table.insert(names, i.Name);
        end;

        return `List of players being recorded: \n • {table.concat(names, `\n • `)}`;
    end
    return
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/blinkServer.lua ---

--[[
    blinkServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context)
  local character = context.Executor.Character

	if not character then
		return "You don't have a character."
	end

  local data = context:GetData()
  local hit = data and data.hit
  if not hit or typeof(hit) ~= "Vector3" then
    return "Internal error"
  end

	character:MoveTo(hit)
  return "" -- prevent clogging up the output
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/getlifestart.lua ---

--[[
    getlifestart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return {
  Name = "getlifestart",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Returns the relative time the specified player's life started",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "player",
      Name = "Player",
      Description = "The player whose life start time to return",
    }
  },
  ClientRun = function(_, player)
    local spawnTime = player:GetAttribute("LifeStart")
    if not spawnTime then
      return `{player.Name}'s life start is unknown`
    end

    local relative = os.time() - spawnTime
    return (`{player.Name}'s life started %dm %ds ago ({DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(spawnTime):FormatUniversalTime("LTS", "en-us")})`):format(
      math.floor(relative / 60) % 60,
      math.floor(relative) % 60
    ) .. "\nNOTE: This is only reset when a player is killed by emergency services or other organisation (i.e. NSEC) and respawns or when a player is booked. NLR rules may include more conditions than this mechanic."
  end
}



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/getspawntime.lua ---

--[[
    getspawntime (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return {
  Name = "getspawntime",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Returns the relative time the specified player's character spawned",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "player",
      Name = "Player",
      Description = "The player whose character spawn time to return",
    }
  },
  ClientRun = function(_, player)
    local char = player.Character
    if not char then
      return `{player.Name} has no character.`
    end
    local spawnTime = char:GetAttribute("Spawned")
    if not spawnTime then
      return `{player.Name}'s spawn time is unknown`
    end

    local relative = os.time() - spawnTime
    return (`{player.Name} spawned %dm %ds ago ({DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(spawnTime):FormatUniversalTime("LTS", "en-us")})`):format(
      math.floor(relative / 60) % 60,
      math.floor(relative) % 60
    )
  end
}

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/grep.lua ---

--[[
    grep (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return {
  Name = "grep",
  Description = "Searches logs",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    function (context)
      return {
        Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("log", {"Commands", "Kills", "Joins", "Leaves", "Teams"}),
        Name = "Log",
        Description = "The type of log you want to view",
      }
    end,
    {
      Type = "string",
      Name = "str"
    }
  }
}



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/grepServer.lua ---

--[[
    grepServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(ctx, log, str)
  local vals = {}
  for value, entry in _G.Aero.Services.LogsService.Logs[log]:IterReversed() do
    if string.find(value, str) then
      table.insert(vals, value)
    end
  end

  if #vals == 0 then
    return "No results"
  else
    return table.concat(vals, "\n")
  end
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/InfoServer.lua ---

--[[
    InfoServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, target)
    local Chat = game:GetService('Chat');
    local hasSafeChat = (not Chat:CanUserChatAsync(target.userId) and true) or (Chat:FilterStringAsync("C7RN", target, target) == "####") or false

    local text = ("%s's account is %d days old. Safechat: "..tostring(hasSafeChat)):format(target.Name, target.AccountAge)
    _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(context.Executor, 'User Info', text, nil, 'Purple');
    return text
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/ingameadmins.lua ---

--[[
    ingameadmins (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local AdminLevels = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.Constants.AdminLevels)
local TableUtil = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.TableUtil)

local NAME_OVERRIDES = {
  HeadAdmin = "Head Admins",
  Moderator = "Moderators",
  Admin = "Admins"
}

local levelMap = {}
for name, level in AdminLevels do
  levelMap[level] = name
end

return {
  Name = "ingameadmins",
  Aliases = {"admins"},
  Description = "Provides a list of in-game admins",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {},
  ClientRun = function(_)
    local admins = TableUtil.Map(TableUtil.Copy(AdminLevels), function()
      return {}
    end)
    admins.Developer = {}

    for _, player in ipairs(Players:GetPlayers()) do
      if player:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then
        table.insert(admins.Developer, player.Name)
        continue
      end

      local adminLevel = player:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") or 0
      if adminLevel > 0 then
        table.insert(admins[levelMap[adminLevel]], player.Name)
      end
    end

    local output = {}
    for i, group in ipairs(levelMap) do
      local groupAdmins = admins[group]
      local name = `{NAME_OVERRIDES[group] or group} ({#groupAdmins})`
      table.insert(output, name)
      table.insert(output, string.rep("-", #name))
      table.insert(output, table.concat(groupAdmins, "\n"))

      -- new line for next group
      if i ~= #levelMap and #groupAdmins > 0 then
        table.insert(output, "")
      end
    end

    local dev = `Developers ({#admins.Developer})`
    table.insert(output, dev)
    table.insert(output, string.rep("-", #dev))
    table.insert(output, table.concat(admins.Developer, "\n"))

    return table.concat(output, "\n")
  end
}

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/MessageServer.lua ---

--[[
    MessageServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, message)
	local plr = context.Executor;
	local FilterStringAsync = _G.Aero.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;	
	local filterResult: TextFilterResult = FilterStringAsync(message, plr.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);

	filterResult = filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();

	_G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.SendAll('ADMIN_MESSAGE',('Message from %s'):format(plr.Name), filterResult);
	return 'Sent message.';
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/pnum.lua ---

--[[
    pnum (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local Teams = game:GetService("Teams")

return {
  Name = "pnum",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Returns the number of players in game",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
  },
  ClientRun = function()
    local output = {}
    local jobs = {}

    for _, team: Team in Teams:GetChildren() do
      if team:IsA("Team") then
        local count = #team:GetPlayers()
        if count < 1 then
          continue
        end
        table.insert(output, `{team.Name} - {count}`)
      end
    end

    for _, player in Players:GetPlayers() do
      local job = player:GetAttribute('CurrentJob')
      local division = player:GetAttribute('Division')

      if player.Team.Name == "Civilian" and division ~= nil and division ~= 'GCPS' then
        jobs[division] = (jobs[division] or 0) + 1
      end
      if job ~= nil then
        jobs[job] = (jobs[job] or 0) + 1
      end
    end

    if #jobs > 0 then
      table.insert(output, "\nCivilian jobs:")
    end
    for job, count in jobs do
      table.insert(output, `{job} - {count}`)
    end

    return `{#Players:GetPlayers()} players:\n` .. table.concat(output, "\n")
  end
}

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Moderator/thruServer.lua ---

--[[
    thruServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Moderator
    Parent: Moderator
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, extra)
	local character = context.Executor.Character

	if not character or not character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
		return "You don't have a character."
	end

  local data = context:GetData()
  local hit = data and data.hit
  if not hit or typeof(hit) ~= "Vector3" then
    return "Internal error"
  end

	local pos = character.HumanoidRootPart.Position
	local diff = (hit - pos)

	character:MoveTo((diff * 2) + (diff.unit * extra) + pos)
	return "" -- prevent clogging the output
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/music/playServer.lua ---

--[[
    playServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → music
    Parent: music
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local SoundService = game:GetService("SoundService")
local MarketplaceService = game:GetService("MarketplaceService")

local function stopMusic()
  for _, v in SoundService:GetChildren() do
    if v.ClassName == "Sound" and v.Name == "COMMAND_SOUND" then
      v:Destroy()
    end
  end
end

return function(_, assetId: number, hint: boolean, loop: boolean, pitch: number, volume: number)
  if assetId <= 0 then
    stopMusic()
    return "Stopped playing music"
  end

  local nowPlaying: string?
  local ok = pcall(function()
    local productInfo = MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(assetId, Enum.InfoType.Asset)
    if productInfo.AssetTypeId == 3 then
      nowPlaying = productInfo.Name
    end
  end)

  if ok and not nowPlaying then
    return "Invalid id"
  end

  local s = Instance.new("Sound")
  s.Name = "COMMAND_SOUND"
  s.SoundId = `rbxassetid://{assetId}`
  s.Volume = volume
  s.Pitch = pitch
  s.Looped = loop
  s.Archivable = false
  stopMusic()
  s.Parent = SoundService

  if hint then
    task.delay(0.5, function()
      _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.SendAll("Now playing", nowPlaying, nil, 'Purple')
    end)
  end
  task.wait(0.5)
  s:Play()

  return `Now playing {nowPlaying}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/POU/protectee.lua ---

--[[
    protectee (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → POU
    Parent: POU
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33

return {
  Name = "protectee",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Command for POU to mark or unmark a person as a protectee",
  Group = "Root",
  Args = {
    function (context)
      return {
        Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("ProtecteeAction", {"add", "remove", "list"}),
        Name = "Action",
        Description = "",
      }
    end,
    function (context)
      local action = context:GetArgument(1):GetValue()
      if action ~= "list" then
        return {
          Type = "player",
          Name = "Player",
          Description = `The player to {action} as a protectee.`,
        }
      end
      return {
        Type = "string",
        Name = "Press enter to continue",
        Optional = true,
      }
    end,
  },

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/POU/protecteeServer.lua ---

--[[
    protecteeServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → POU
    Parent: POU
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
return function(_, action, player)
  if action == "list" then
    local output = {}
    for _, plr in Players:GetPlayers() do
      if plr:GetAttribute("Protectee") then
        table.insert(output, plr.Name)
      end
    end
    return `{#output} players:\n`.. table.concat(output, "\n")
  elseif action == "add" then
    if player:GetAttribute("Protectee") then
      return `{player.Name} is already a protectee.`
    end
    player:SetAttribute("Protectee", true)
    return `{player.Name} is now a protectee.`
  elseif action == "remove" then
    if not player:GetAttribute("Protectee") then
      return `{player.Name} is not a protectee.`
    end
    player:SetAttribute("Protectee", nil)
    return `{player.Name} is no-longer a protectee.`
  end
  return "Unknown action type"
end

  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "playerIds",
      Name = "Players",
      Description = "The players to serverban",

      Optional = true,

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/punishment/banServer.lua ---

--[[
    banServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → punishment
    Parent: punishment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

return function(ctx, playerIds, reason)
  reason = reason or "Unspecified reason"

  local FilterStringAsync = _G.Aero.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
	local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(reason, ctx.Executor.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);
	filterResult = filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();

  local executorLevel = ctx.Executor:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") or 0
  if ctx.Executor:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then
    executorLevel = 9
  end

  for _, playerId in playerIds do
    local player = Players:GetPlayerByUserId(playerId)
    if player then
      local playerLevel = player:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") or 0
      if player:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then
        playerLevel = 9
      end

      if playerLevel > executorLevel then
        ctx:Reply(`Could not serverban {player.Name} as they have a higher admin level.`)
        continue
      end

      if player == ctx.Executor then
        ctx:Reply("Banning yourself is unwise.")
        continue
      end
    end

    ctx:GetStore("Bans")[playerId] = filterResult
    if player then
      player:SetAttribute("Moderated", true)
      player:Kick(`Server banned — {reason}`)
      _G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.SendAll('Notification', 'Player Banned', `{player.Name} has been banned from this server.`, nil, 'Purple')
    end
  end

  return `Serverbanned {#playerIds} players for reason {filterResult}`
end

--[[
    kick (ModuleScript)

    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33

return {
  Name = "kick",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Removes the specified player from the server",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "players",
      Name = "Players",
      Description = "The players to kick",
    },
    {
      Type = "string",
      Name = "Reason",
      Description = "The reason to be shown to the player(s)",
      Optional = true,
    }
  },
}



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/punishment/kickServer.lua ---

--[[
    kickServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → punishment
    Parent: punishment
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(ctx, players, reason)
  reason = reason or "Unspecified reason"

  local FilterStringAsync = _G.Aero.Modules.Filter.FilterStringAsync;
	local filterResult = FilterStringAsync(reason, ctx.Executor.UserId, Enum.TextFilterContext.PublicChat);
	filterResult = filterResult:GetNonChatStringForBroadcastAsync();

  local executorLevel = ctx.Executor:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") or 0
  if ctx.Executor:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then
    executorLevel = 9
  end

  local playerNames = {}
  for _, player in players do
    local playerLevel = player:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") or 0
    if player:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then
      playerLevel = 9
    end

    if playerLevel > executorLevel then
      ctx:Reply(`Could not kick {player.Name} as they have a higher admin level.`)
      continue
    end

    player:SetAttribute("Moderated", true)
    player:Kick(`Moderation — {filterResult}`)
    _G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.SendAll('Notification', 'Player Kicked', `{player.Name} has been kicked from this server.`, nil, 'Purple')
    table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
  end

  return `Kicked {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} for reason {filterResult}`
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Root/announceshutdownServer.lua ---

--[[
    announceshutdownServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Root
    Parent: Root
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
return function(ctx)
    local executor = ctx.Executor;

    local aero = _G.Aero;
    local services = aero.Services;

    services.NetworkService.SendAll('ServerShutdownMessage', executor);

    Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(function(player)
        player:Kick('This server is being shutdown by a developer. Please rejoin in approximately 2 minutes.');
    end);

    task.delay(2, function()
        for i = 60, 1, -1 do
            services.NotificationService.SendAll('Shutdown Timer', `{i}`, nil, 'Purple');
            task.wait(1);
        end;
    end)

    return "Command executed"
end;

local CollectionService = game:GetService('CollectionService');

return function(context, target)
	local plr = context.Executor;

    local char = target.Character;
    if not char then return "Target has no character"; end;

    local rootPart = char:FindFirstChild('HumanoidRootPart');

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Root/billboard/gcbServer.lua ---

--[[
    gcbServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Root → billboard
    Parent: billboard
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(ctx)
  local billboard = game.CollectionService:GetTagged("Billboard")[1]
  local prefix = "https://www.roblox.com/asset-thumbnail/image?assetId="
  local uri = billboard.BillboardGUI.MainFrame.UIPageLayout.CurrentPage and billboard.BillboardGUI.MainFrame.UIPageLayout.CurrentPage.Image
  if not uri then
    return "No image running"
  end
  local stop = uri:find("&")
  local id = uri:sub(#prefix + 1, stop - 1)
  local name = game.MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(id).Name

  local pub, exp

  for _, v in _G.Aero.Services.Environment.BillboardService.ImageData do
    if v.Image == uri then
      pub = if typeof(v.Player) == "Instance" then v.Player.Name else game:GetService("Players"):GetNameFromUserIdAsync(v.Player)
      exp = DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(v.Expiry):FormatUniversalTime("ll LT", "en-gb")
      break
    end
  end

  return `{id} - {name}\nPublished by {pub}\nExpires {exp}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Root/ChangePrisonTimeServer.lua ---

--[[
    ChangePrisonTimeServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Root
    Parent: Root
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
-- Change Prison Time Server
-- Khizzer
-- January 7, 2022

return function(context, target, time)
	local plr = context.Executor;

    local prisonService = _G.Aero.Services.PrisonService;
    local inmate = prisonService:GetPrisoner(target);

    if time == nil then
        if target.Team == game.Teams.Prisoner then
            target:SetAttribute('ReleaseFromPrison', true);
            return string.format('Successfully cleared prison time for player: %s', target.Name)
        else
            return 'User is not a prisoner.'
        end;
    else
        _G.Aero.Modules.DataService.Set(target, 'PrisonTime', time);
        if inmate then
            inmate:SetTime(time);
            return string.format('Successfully changed prison time for player: %s', target.Name)
        else
            if time == 0 then return 'User is not a prisoner.' end
            prisonService.AddPrisonerSignal:Fire(target, time);
            return string.format('Successfully added prison time for player: %s', target.Name), nil, 'Purple'
        end;
    end;
end

-- Change Weather
-- Khizzer
-- January 7, 2022

local WeatherTemplates = {
    ['Light Rain'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 3;
            Density = 0.3;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = true;
            IntensityRatio = 0.5;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.8;
            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Probability = 0.3;
    };
    ['Heavy Rain'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 3;
            Density = 0.3;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = true;
            IntensityRatio = 0.7;

        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.8;
            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Probability = 0.1
    };
    --Make cloudy weather
    ['Cloudy'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 0;
            Density = 0.2;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = false;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.5;
            Cover = 0.6;
        };
        Probability = 0.5;
    };
    ['Really Cloudy'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 0;
            Density = 0.2;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = false;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.589;
            Cover = 0.685;
        };
        Probability = 0.3;
    };
    ['Overcast'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 0;
            Density = 0.2;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = false;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.63;
            Cover = 0.822;
        };
        Probability = 0.25;
    };
    ['Clear'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 0;
            Density = 0.2;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(200, 200, 200);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = false;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.5;
            Cover = 0.47;
        };
        Probability = 0.6;
    };
    ['Snowstorm'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 3;
            Density = 0.4;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(216, 216, 216);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = true;
            IntensityRatio = 0.85;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.8;
            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Probability = 0.4;
        Snow = true;
    };
    ['Light Snow'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 3;
            Density = 0.3;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(216, 216, 216);
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = true;
            IntensityRatio = 0.5;
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.8;
            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Probability = 0.4;
        Snow = true;
    };
    ['Fog'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 3;
            Density = 0.45;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150);
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.8;
            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = false;
        };
        Probability = 0.15;
    };
    ['Heavy Fog'] = {
        Atmosphere = {
            Haze = 3;
            Density = 0.5;
            Color = Color3.fromRGB(150, 150, 150);
        };
        Clouds = {
            Density = 0.8;
            Cover = 0.8;
        };
        Rain = {
            Enabled = false;
        };
        Probability = 0.1;
    };
}

return function(context, weather, tweenTime)
	local plr = context.Executor;

	local NetworkService = _G.Aero.Services.NetworkService;
	local WeatherService = _G.Aero.Services.Environment.WeatherService;
	local NotificationService = _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService;

	if weather == 'Thunderstorm' then
		NetworkService.SendAll('onWeatherChange', WeatherTemplates['Heavy Rain'], tweenTime);
		WeatherService.EnableThunder(true);
	else
		NetworkService.SendAll('onWeatherChange', WeatherTemplates[weather], tweenTime);
		WeatherService.EnableThunder(false);
	end

	NotificationService.Send(plr, 'Weather Changed', string.format('Successfully changed the weather to: %s', weather), nil, 'Purple')
	return string.format('Successfully changed the weather to: %s', weather);
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Root/InsertServer.lua ---

--[[
    InsertServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Root
    Parent: Root
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
-- Insert Server
-- Khizzer
-- August 8, 2023

local InsertService = game:GetService('InsertService');

local blacklist = {74385399}

return function(context, insertId, isCar)
    local plr = context.Executor;

    if table.find(blacklist, insertId) then
        return "This ID is prohibited."
    end

    local model = InsertService:LoadAsset(insertId);

    local asset = model:GetChildren()[1] :: Instance;

    if asset:FindFirstChild('CarServer') or isCar then
        asset.ModelStreamingMode = Enum.ModelStreamingMode.Persistent;
        asset.Parent = workspace.Cars;
        plr.Car.Value = asset;
        asset:SetAttribute('Owner', plr.Name);

        local config = asset:FindFirstChild('Config')
        local state = config and config:FindFirstChild('State')
        local locked = state and state:FindFirstChild('Locked')
        if locked ~= nil then
            locked.Value = true
        end
    else
        asset.Parent = if asset:IsA("Tool") then plr.Backpack else workspace;
    end;

    if not asset:IsA("Tool") then
        table.insert(context:GetStore('Inserted'), asset);
        asset:SetAttribute("Inserted", true);
    else
        asset:SetAttribute("DoNotRemove", true);
        asset:SetAttribute("DoNotSave", true);
        asset:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `Inserted by {context.Executor.Name} ({DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us')})`);
    end
    if asset:IsA("Model") and not asset:IsA("Tool") then
        asset:PivotTo(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
    end

    model:Destroy();

    return "Inserted"
end;
