options.ShouldReserveServer = true
options:SetTeleportData({
    ssdisable = true
})

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Root/ResetInventoryServer.lua ---

--[[
    ResetInventoryServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Root
    Parent: Root
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, userId)
    local ProfileDataService = _G.Aero.Modules.ProfileDataService;
    local WebUtil = _G.Aero.Modules.WebUtil;

    local ProfileStore = ProfileDataService:GetProfileStore();

    local username = game:GetService('Players'):GetNameFromUserIdAsync(userId)
    local profileKey = `Player_{userId}`;

    ProfileStore:GlobalUpdateProfileAsync(profileKey, function(globalUpdates)
        globalUpdates:AddActiveUpdate({
            ResetInventory = true;
        })
    end)

    WebUtil.SendJSON("https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1109478672429220002/ZCZ7wnLdHzgX9JgF8nPujNr0nCEznxwv2dYB0SZKyEJbxYJpOhb6_pE-uSAm8Ov6_yuf", {
        embeds = {
            {
                title = "Inventory Reset",
                fields = {
                    {
                        name = "Developer";
                        value = context.Executor.Name;
                    },
                    {
                        name = "Target";
                        value = username;
                    },
                },
                footer = {
                    text = "This will take effect the next time they join the game."
                }
            }
        }
    })

    return 'Global update applied';
end;

			Description = "The license plate of the vehicle. Defaults to nothing.",
			Default = ""
		},
		{
			Type = "color3",
			Name = "colour",
			Description = "The colour of the vehicle.",
			Optional = true,
		}
	}
}



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/Root/SpawnCarServer.lua ---

--[[
    SpawnCarServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → Root
    Parent: Root
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(context, carToSpawn, owner: Player?, plate: string?, color: Color3?)
	local plr = context.Executor

	local clone = carToSpawn:Clone()

	clone.ModelStreamingMode = Enum.ModelStreamingMode.Persistent
	clone:SetAttribute("SpawnedCar", true)
	clone.Parent = workspace.Cars
	clone:PivotTo(plr.Character:GetPivot());
	(if owner then owner else plr).Car.Value = clone
	clone:SetAttribute('Owner', if owner then owner.Name else plr.Name)

	local config = clone:FindFirstChild('Config')
	if config then
		local state = config:FindFirstChild('State')
		local locked = state and state:FindFirstChild('Locked')
		if locked ~= nil then
			locked.Value = true
		end

		if plate and config:FindFirstChild("LicensePlate") then
			config.LicensePlate.Value = plate
			clone:SetAttribute("LicensePlate", plate)
		end

		if color and config:FindFirstChild("CanBePainted") and config.CanBePainted.Value then
			clone:SetAttribute("Color", color)
			_G.Aero.Services.CarModificationService:PaintCar(clone, color)
		end
	end

	local spawnerSettings = config and config:FindFirstChild("SpawnerSettings")
	local ID = spawnerSettings and spawnerSettings:FindFirstChild("ID")
	if ID then
		ID:Clone().Parent = config;
		-- (if owner then owner else plr):SetAttribute('LastVehicle', ID.Value)
	end
	if spawnerSettings then
		spawnerSettings:Destroy()
	end

	return ("Spawned car: %s"):format(carToSpawn.Name)
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/scr/releasefromprisonServer.lua ---

--[[
    releasefromprisonServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr
    Parent: scr
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
return function(ctx, userId)
  if Players:GetPlayerByUserId(userId) then
    return `Player is in game, use setprisontime instead.`
  end

  local ProfileDataService = _G.Aero.Modules.ProfileDataService;
  local ProfileStore = ProfileDataService:GetProfileStore();

  ProfileStore:GlobalUpdateProfileAsync(`Player_{userId}`, function(globalUpdates)
      globalUpdates:AddActiveUpdate({
        ReleaseFromPrison = true;
      })
  end)

  return 'Global update applied';
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/scr/relServer.lua ---

--[[
    relServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr
    Parent: scr
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local parts = "Head Left Right"

return function(ctx, players)
  for _, suspect in players do
    local suspectCharacter = suspect.Character

    local handcuffedBy = suspect:GetAttribute("HandcuffedBy")
    suspect:SetAttribute("HandcuffedBy", nil)
    suspect:SetAttribute("InZipties", nil)
    _G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(suspect, "SetInventoryEnabled", true)

    local targetToolParent = suspect.Backpack

    if suspect:GetAttribute("Ragdoll") then
      targetToolParent = _G.Aero.Services.PlayerService:GetPlayerSessionStorage(suspect).DeathToolStorage
    end

    for _, v in suspect:GetChildren() do
      if v:IsA("Tool") then
        v.Parent = targetToolParent
      end
    end

    suspect:SetAttribute("GrabbedBy", nil)
    suspectCharacter.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false

    _G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(suspect, "SuspectCuffAnimation", false)

    local plr = Players:FindFirstChild(handcuffedBy)
    if plr then
      _G.Aero.Services.NetworkService.Send(plr, "OfficerCuffAnimation", false)
      if plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint') then
          plr.Character.Torso:FindFirstChildOfClass('WeldConstraint'):Destroy();
          for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
              if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
                  v.Massless = false;
                  v.CanCollide = false;
              end;
          end;
      end;
    end

    for _,v in next, suspectCharacter:GetDescendants() do
      if v:IsA('BasePart') and parts:find(v.Name) then
          v.Massless = false;
          v.CanCollide = false;
      end;
      if v:IsA('BasePart') then
          v.CollisionGroupId = 0;
      end
    end;

    suspectCharacter.Humanoid.JumpPower = 50
  end
end

--[[
    resetmoneyServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr
    Parent: scr
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ds = game:GetService('DataStoreService'):GetOrderedDataStore('MoneyData')
return function(ctx, userId)
  local ProfileDataService = _G.Aero.Modules.ProfileDataService;
  local WebUtil = _G.Aero.Modules.WebUtil;

  local ProfileStore = ProfileDataService:GetProfileStore();

  local username = game:GetService('Players'):GetNameFromUserIdAsync(userId)
  local profileKey = `Player_{userId}`;
  local money = ds:GetAsync(userId)

  ProfileStore:GlobalUpdateProfileAsync(profileKey, function(globalUpdates)
      globalUpdates:AddActiveUpdate({
          ResetMoney = true;
      })
  end)
  ds:SetAsync(userId, 0)

  WebUtil.SendJSON("https://webhook.lewisakura.moe/api/webhooks/1109478672429220002/ZCZ7wnLdHzgX9JgF8nPujNr0nCEznxwv2dYB0SZKyEJbxYJpOhb6_pE-uSAm8Ov6_yuf", {
      embeds = {
          {
              title = "Money Reset",
              fields = {
                  {
                      name = "Developer";
                      value = ctx.Executor.Name;
                  },
                  {
                      name = "Target";
                      value = username;
                  },
                  {
                    name = "Money";
                    value = money;
                  }
              },
              footer = {
                  text = "This will take effect the next time they join the game."
              }
          }
      }
  })

  return 'Global update applied';
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/scr/richestServer.lua ---

--[[
    richestServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr
    Parent: scr
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ds = game:GetService('DataStoreService'):GetOrderedDataStore('MoneyData')

local function format_int(number)
  local i, j, minus, int, fraction = tostring(number):find('([-]?)(%d+)([.]?%d*)')
  int = int:reverse():gsub("(%d%d%d)", "%1,")
  return minus .. int:reverse():gsub("^,", "") .. fraction
end

return function(ctx, count)
  local top = ds:GetSortedAsync(false, count):GetCurrentPage()
  local s = `{count} richest players`
  local i = 0
  for _, x in ipairs(top) do
    local username
    if x.key:sub(#x.key, #x.key) == 'D' then
      username = game:GetService("Players"):GetNameFromUserIdAsync(x.key:sub(1, #x.key-1)) .. " (Dev)"
    else
      i += 1
      username = game:GetService("Players"):GetNameFromUserIdAsync(x.key)
    end
    s ..= `\n{i}. {username} - {format_int(x.value)}`
  end
  return s
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/scr/sl/slServer.lua ---

--[[
    slServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr → sl
    Parent: sl
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local playerStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("session_log")

local function formatDate(time: DateTime)
  return time:FormatUniversalTime("ll LT", "en-gb")
end

local function format_int(number)
  local i, j, minus, int, fraction = tostring(number):find('([-]?)(%d+)([.]?%d*)')
  int = int:reverse():gsub("(%d%d%d)", "%1,")
  return minus .. int:reverse():gsub("^,", "") .. fraction
end

local function formatTime(seconds)
  if seconds > 3600 then
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local remainingSeconds = seconds - (hours * 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor(remainingSeconds / 60)
    return `{format_int(hours)} hours, {format_int(minutes)} minutes`
  elseif seconds > 60 then
    return `{format_int(math.floor(seconds / 60))} minutes`
  else
    return `{format_int(seconds)} seconds`
  end
end

return function(_, playerId)
  local data = playerStore:GetAsync(playerId)
  if not data then
    return "No data found."
  end

  local output = {}
  for _, v in data do
    local join = formatDate(DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(v[1]))
    local leave = v[4] and formatDate(DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(v[4]))

    local str = `Joined {join}, {v[3]} players in game.`
    if leave then
      local duration = v[4] - v[1]
      str ..= ` Left {leave}, {v[5]} players. ({formatTime(duration)})`
    end
    table.insert(output, str)
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{#data} joins since 14 Jan 2024:{sep}{table.concat(output, sep)}`
end

--[[
    timeServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr → sl
    Parent: sl
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")
local ds = game:GetService('DataStoreService'):GetOrderedDataStore('InGameTime')

local function formatDate(time: DateTime)
  return time:FormatUniversalTime("ll LT", "en-gb")
end

local function format_int(number)
  local i, j, minus, int, fraction = tostring(number):find('([-]?)(%d+)([.]?%d*)')
  int = int:reverse():gsub("(%d%d%d)", "%1,")
  return minus .. int:reverse():gsub("^,", "") .. fraction
end

local function formatTime(seconds)
  if seconds > 3600 then
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local remainingSeconds = seconds - (hours * 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor(remainingSeconds / 60)
    return `{format_int(hours)} hours, {format_int(minutes)} minutes`
  else
    return `{format_int(math.floor(seconds / 60))} minutes`
  end
end

return function(_, playerId)
  local data = ds:GetAsync(playerId)
  if not data then
    return "No data found."
  end

  local duration = formatTime(data)
  local username = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(playerId)

  return `{username} has spent {duration} in game since 10 Jan 2024`
end

--[[
    tlbServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → scr
    Parent: scr
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33

local ds = game:GetService('DataStoreService'):GetOrderedDataStore('InGameTime')

local function format_int(number)
  local i, j, minus, int, fraction = tostring(number):find('([-]?)(%d+)([.]?%d*)')
  int = int:reverse():gsub("(%d%d%d)", "%1,")
  return minus .. int:reverse():gsub("^,", "") .. fraction
end

local function formatTime(seconds)
  if seconds > 3600 then
    local hours = math.floor(seconds / 3600)
    local remainingSeconds = seconds - (hours * 3600)
    local minutes = math.floor(remainingSeconds / 60)
    return `{format_int(hours)} hours, {format_int(minutes)} minutes`
  else
    return `{format_int(math.floor(seconds / 60))} minutes`
  end
end

return function(ctx, count)
  local top = ds:GetSortedAsync(false, count):GetCurrentPage()
  local s = `{count} players with highest in-game time since 10 Jan 2024`
  for i, x in ipairs(top) do
    local username = game:GetService("Players"):GetNameFromUserIdAsync(x.key)
    s ..= `\n{i}. {username} - {formatTime(x.value)}`
  end
  return s
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/sec/corServer.lua ---

--[[
    corServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → sec
    Parent: sec
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local playerStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("vHPlayer")
local hashStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("vHashes")

return function(ctx, playerId)
  local hashesData = playerStore:GetAsync(playerId)
  if not hashesData then
    return "No data found."
  end

  local names = {}
  local userIds = {}

  local correlationData = {}
  for hash, set in hashesData do
    local ok, plrData = pcall(hashStore.GetAsync, hashStore, hash)
    if not ok then
      ctx:Reply(`Failed to load hash {hash}\n{plrData}`)
      continue
    end
    if not plrData then
      continue
    end
    local players = {}
    for playerId in plrData do
      local display = `#{playerId}`
      pcall(function()
        if names[playerId] then
          display = names[playerId]
          return
        end
        local name = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(tonumber(playerId))
        if typeof(name) ~= "string" then
          return
        end
        display = name
        names[playerId] = name
      end)
      table.insert(players, display)
      userIds[playerId] = true
    end
    table.insert(correlationData, {
      compare = set[1], -- first_join
      users = players,
      hash = hash,
    })
  end

  table.sort(correlationData, function(a, b)
    return a.compare < b.compare
  end)

  local output = {}
  for _, v in correlationData do
    table.insert(output, `{v.hash} - {table.concat(v.users, ", ")}`)
  end

  local u = {}
  for id in userIds do
    if names[id] then
      table.insert(u, names[id])
    else
      table.insert(u, `#{id}`)
    end
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{#u} users: {table.concat(u, ", ")}\n{#output} hashes:{sep}{table.concat(output, sep)}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/sec/ghServer.lua ---

--[[
    ghServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → sec
    Parent: sec
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local playerStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("vHPlayer")

local function formatTime(time: DateTime)
  return time:FormatUniversalTime("ll LT", "en-gb")
end

return function(_, playerId)
  local data = playerStore:GetAsync(playerId)
  if not data then
    return "No data found."
  end

  local hashes = {}
  for hash, set in data do
    table.insert(hashes, {
      hash = hash,
      data = set
    })
  end

  table.sort(hashes, function(a, b)
    return a.data[1] < b.data[1]
  end)

  local output = {}
  for _, v in hashes do
    local firstJoin = formatTime(DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(v.data[1]))
    local lastJoin = formatTime(DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(v.data[2]))

    table.insert(output, `{v.hash} - First join {firstJoin}, last join {lastJoin}`)
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{#output} hashes found:{sep}{table.concat(output, sep)}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/sec/lhServer.lua ---

--[[
    lhServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → sec
    Parent: sec
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local DataStoreService = game:GetService("DataStoreService")
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

local hashStore = DataStoreService:GetDataStore("vHashes")

local function formatTime(time: DateTime)
  return time:FormatUniversalTime("ll LT", "en-gb")
end

return function(_, hash)
  local data = hashStore:GetAsync(hash)
  if not data then
    return "No data found."
  end

  local output = {}
  for playerId, set in data do
    local firstJoin = formatTime(DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(set[1]))
    local lastJoin = formatTime(DateTime.fromUnixTimestamp(set[2]))
    local display = `#{playerId}`

    pcall(function()
      local name = Players:GetNameFromUserIdAsync(tonumber(playerId))
      if typeof(name) ~= "string" then
        return
      end
      display = name
    end)

    table.insert(output, `{display} ({playerId}) - First join {firstJoin}, last join {lastJoin}`)
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{#output} users found:{sep}{table.concat(output, sep)}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/team/setteam.lua ---

--[[
    setteam (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → team
    Parent: team
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local TableUtil = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.TableUtil)
local divisionStorage = ReplicatedStorage.Divisions

return {
  Name = "setteam",
  Aliases = {},
  Description = "Changes the team of the target player",
  Group = "HeadAdmin",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "players",
      Name = "Players",
      Description = "The players whose team to change",
    },
    {
      Type = "team",
      Name = "Team",
      Description = "The team to set the players to",
    },
    function (context)
      local team = context:GetArgument(2):GetValue()
      local teamDivisions = team and divisionStorage:FindFirstChild(team.Name)
      if not teamDivisions then
        return {
          Type = "string",
          Name = "Press enter to continue",
          Optional = true,
        }
      end

      return {
        Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("division", TableUtil.Map(TableUtil.Filter(teamDivisions:GetChildren(), function(x)
          return x.Name ~= "GCPS"
        end), function(d)
          return d.Name
        end)),
        Name = "Division",
        Description = `The specific division within {team.Name} to use, leave blank to use the default division.`,
        Optional = true,
      }
    end,
  },
}



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/team/setteamServer.lua ---

--[[
    setteamServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → team
    Parent: team
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")

local divisionStorage = ReplicatedStorage.Divisions

return function(ctx, players, team, d)
  local ToolService = _G.Aero.Services.ToolService
  local GangService = _G.Aero.Services.GangService

  local divisions = divisionStorage:FindFirstChild(team.Name)
  local division = divisions and d and divisions:FindFirstChild(d)

  local playerNames = {}

	for _, player in pairs(players) do
    if player.Team.Name == "Civilian" then
      ToolService:SaveCivilianTools(player)
    elseif player.Team.Name ~= "Civilian" and team.Name == "Civilian" then
      player:SetAttribute('GiveBackCivilianTools', true)
    end
    if player.Team.Name == "Civilian" and team.Name ~= "Civilian" then
      GangService:RemovePlayer(player)
    end

		player.Team = team

    if division then
      player:SetAttribute("Division", division.Name)
    else
      player:SetAttribute("Division", nil)
    end

    player:LoadCharacter()
		table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
    _G.Aero.Services.LogsService:AddLog('Teams', `{player.Name} set to {(division or team).Name} by {ctx.Executor}`)

		if player ~= ctx.Executor then
			_G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Team change', 'Your team has been changed by an admin.', nil, 'Purple')
		end
	end

  return `Changed {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} to be {(division or team).Name}`
end

      Type = "players",
      Name = "Players",

          if context.Executor.UserId ~= 25198607 and context.Executor.UserId ~= 47890485 then

          end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/tools/analysetoolsServer.lua ---

--[[
    analysetoolsServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → tools
    Parent: tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(_, target: Player)
  if not target:FindFirstChild("Backpack") then
    return `{target.Name} has no tools`
  end

  local tools = {}

  if target.Character and target.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool") then
    local tool = target.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool")
    if tool:GetAttribute("ToolSource") ~= nil then
      table.insert(tools, `Equipped: {tool.Name} — {tool:GetAttribute("ToolSource")}`)
    end
  end

  for _, tool in target.Backpack:GetChildren() do
    if tool:IsA("Tool") and tool:GetAttribute("ToolSource") ~= nil then
      table.insert(tools, `{tool.Name} — {tool:GetAttribute("ToolSource")}`)
    end
  end
  for _, tool in target:GetChildren() do
    if tool:IsA("Tool") and tool:GetAttribute("ToolSource") ~= nil then
      table.insert(tools, `{tool.Name} — {tool:GetAttribute("ToolSource")}`)
    end
  end

  if #tools == 0 then
    return `{target.Name} has no applicable tools`
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{target.Name} has {#tools} applicable tools:{sep}{table.concat(tools, sep)}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/tools/btoolsServer.lua ---

--[[
    btoolsServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → tools
    Parent: tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
-- btools Server
-- Khizzer
-- August 8, 2023


local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage");

local SERVER_ASSETS = ServerStorage.ServerAssets;
local F3X_DEPENDENCIES = SERVER_ASSETS['F3X Dependencies'];

return function(ctx, plr)
	local F3X = Instance.new("Tool");
	F3X.GripPos = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0.4);
	F3X.CanBeDropped = false;
	F3X.ManualActivationOnly = false;
	F3X.RequiresHandle = false;
	F3X.ToolTip = "Building Tools by F3X";
	F3X.Name = "Building Tools";

	local clonedDeps = F3X_DEPENDENCIES:Clone()
	for _, BaseScript in clonedDeps:GetDescendants() do
		if BaseScript:IsA("BaseScript") then
			BaseScript.Disabled = false
		end
	end
	for _, Child in clonedDeps:GetChildren() do
		Child.Parent = F3X
	end
	clonedDeps:Destroy()
	F3X.Handle:Destroy()

    local backpack = plr:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")

    if backpack then
			local date = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us');
        local clone = F3X:Clone()
				clone.Parent = backpack
				clone:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `Spawned by {ctx.Executor.Name} for {plr.Name} ({date})`);
        clone:SetAttribute("DoNotSave", true)
        clone:SetAttribute("DoNotRemove", true)
    end

	return `Successfully gave btools to {plr.Name}`;
end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/tools/cleartoolsServer.lua ---

--[[
    cleartoolsServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → tools
    Parent: tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(ctx, players)
  local playerNames = {}
  for _, player in players do
    if not player:FindFirstChild("Backpack") then
      continue
    end

    local removedTools = false
    for _, tool in player.Backpack:GetChildren() do
      if tool:IsA("Tool") then
        removedTools = true
        tool:Destroy()
      end
    end

    if removedTools then
      table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
      _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Tools', `{ctx.Executor} cleared your tools`, nil, 'Purple');
    end
  end

  return `Removed tools from {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")}`
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/tools/givetoolServer.lua ---

--[[
    givetoolServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → tools
    Parent: tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ServerStorage = game:GetService("ServerStorage")
local TOOL_STORAGE = ServerStorage;

return function(context, targets, toolName)
    local tool = TOOL_STORAGE:FindFirstChild(toolName)
    if not tool or not tool:IsA("Tool") then
        return "No such tool"
    end;

    local date = DateTime.now():FormatUniversalTime('L', 'en-us');
    local playerNames = {}
    for _, player in targets do
        local newTool = tool:Clone();
        newTool.Parent = player.Backpack;
        newTool:SetAttribute('ToolSource', `Spawned by {context.Executor.Name} for {player.Name} ({date})`);
        newTool:SetAttribute("DoNotSave", true); -- This is normally the case, but we're doing it here just to be safe
        table.insert(playerNames, player.Name)
        _G.Aero.Services.NotificationService.Send(player, 'Tools', `{context.Executor} gave you {toolName}`, nil, 'Purple');
    end

    return `Gave {table.concat(playerNames, ", ")} tool {toolName}`
end

      Description = "The name of the tool to be removed. Surround with \"quote marks\" if the tool name includes spaces.",

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/tools/removetoolServer.lua ---

--[[
    removetoolServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → tools
    Parent: tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(_, player, toolName, limit)
  local toolsRemoved = 0
  local toolsFound = 0

  local backpack = player:FindFirstChild("Backpack")
  if not backpack then
    return "Player has no backpack"
  end

  local function clear(container)
    for _, tool in container:GetChildren() do
      if tool:IsA("Tool") and tool.Name == toolName then
        toolsFound += 1
        if limit and toolsRemoved >= limit then
          continue
        end

        tool:Destroy()
        toolsRemoved += 1
      end
    end
  end

  clear(backpack)
  clear(player)
  if player.Character then
    clear(player.Character)
  end

  if (toolsRemoved ~= toolsFound) or limit then
    return `Removed {toolsRemoved} of {toolsFound} matching tools`
  else
    return `Removed {toolsRemoved} matching tools`
  end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/tools/viewtoolsServer.lua ---

--[[
    viewtoolsServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → tools
    Parent: tools
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
return function(_, target: Player)
  if not target:FindFirstChild("Backpack") then
    return `{target.Name} has no tools`
  end

  local tools = {}

  if target.Character and target.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool") then
    local tool = target.Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Tool")
    table.insert(tools, `Equipped: {tool.Name}`)
  end

  for _, tool in target.Backpack:GetChildren() do
    if tool:IsA("Tool") then
      table.insert(tools, tool.Name)
    end
  end
  for _, tool in target:GetChildren() do
    if tool:IsA("Tool") then
      table.insert(tools, tool.Name)
    end
  end

  if #tools == 0 then
    return `{target.Name} has no tools`
  end

  local sep = `\n • `
  return `{target.Name} has {#tools} tools:{sep}{table.concat(tools, sep)}`
end

  Description = "Sets your camera to view another player",
  Group = "Moderator",
  Args = {
    {
      Type = "player",
      Name = "Player",
      Description = "The player to view",
      Optional = true,
    }
  },
  AutoExec = {
    'alias "unview|Resets your camera back to you" view',
    'alias "rv|Resets your camera back to you" view',
  },
  ClientRun = function(ctx, player)
    if not player then
      player = ctx.Executor
    end

    local character = player.Character
		local humanoid = character and character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
		local camera = workspace.CurrentCamera

    if not humanoid then
			return `{player.Name} has no character.`
		end

		if not camera then
			return "You have no camera."
		end

		camera.CameraSubject = humanoid
		return nil -- hand over to server
  end
}

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/whitelist/slockServer.lua ---

--[[
    slockServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → whitelist
    Parent: whitelist
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
_G.ServerLocked = false

return function(ctx, enabled)
  if enabled == nil then
    return `Server lock is {if _G.ServerLocked then "enabled" else "disabled"}`
  end

  local action = if enabled then "enabled" else "disabled"
  if (enabled and _G.ServerLocked) or (not enabled and not _G.ServerLocked) then
    return `Server lock is already {action}`
  end

  warn(`{ctx.Executor} has {action} server lock`)
  _G.ServerLocked = enabled
  return `Server lock has been {action}`
end

  Group = "Admin",
  Args = {
    function (context)
      return {
        Type = context.Cmdr.Util.MakeEnumType("whitelistAction", {"add", "remove", "list"}),
        Name = "Action",
        Description = "",
      }
    end,
    function (context)
      local action = context:GetArgument(1):GetValue()
      if action ~= "list" then
        return {
          Type = "playerId",
          Name = "Player",
          Description = `The player to {action} from the whitelist; supports offline players.`,
        }
      end

        Optional = true,
      }
    end,
  },

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Commands/whitelist/whitelistServer.lua ---

--[[
    whitelistServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Commands → whitelist
    Parent: whitelist
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local Players = game:GetService("Players")

_G.Whitelist = {}

local function getUsername(playerId)
  if Players:GetPlayerByUserId(playerId) then
    return Players:GetPlayerByUserId(playerId).Name
  end
  local ok, res = pcall(Players.GetNameFromUserIdAsync, Players, playerId)
  if ok then
    return res
  end
  return `Player {playerId}`
end

return function(_, action, playerId)
  if action == "list" then
    local output = {}
    for plr in _G.Whitelist do
      local name = getUsername(plr)
      table.insert(output, name)
    end
    return `{#_G.Whitelist} players:\n`.. table.concat(output, "\n")
  elseif action == "add" then
    if _G.Whitelist[playerId] then
      return "Player is already whitelisted"
    end
    _G.Whitelist[playerId] = true
    return "Added to whitelist"
  elseif action == "remove" then
    if not _G.Whitelist[playerId] then
      return "Player is not whitelisted."
    end
    _G.Whitelist[playerId] = nil
    return "Removed from whitelist"
  end
  return "Unknown action type"
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Hooks/BeforeRun.lua ---

--[[
    BeforeRun (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Hooks
    Parent: Hooks
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService('ReplicatedStorage');
local RunService = game:GetService('RunService');
local AdminLevels = require(ReplicatedStorage.Aero.Shared.Constants.AdminLevels)

local GroupMaps = {
  Help = "Moderator",
  DefaultDebug = "Moderator",
  DefaultUtil = "Moderator",
}

local RemapCommands = {
  teleport = "Moderator",

  version = "Root",
  fetch = "Root",
}

local Properties
if RunService:IsClient() then
	local Comm = require(ReplicatedStorage.Packages.Comm)
	local ClientComm = Comm.ClientComm.new(ReplicatedStorage, false, "Specialist")
	Properties = {
		IsGCPS = ClientComm:GetProperty("IsGCPS")
	}
end

-- these are the only commands that should run automatically (i.e. probably before the permissions have loaded)
local PublicCommands = { "alias", "run", "run-lines", "run-if", "var" }

-- Scripter permissions require isDeveloper + a whitelist, which is just... scripters
local Scripters = {25198607, 47890485, 48509356}

local PERM_ERR = "You don't have permission to run this command"

-- this is a gross mess and I want to redo it at some point
return function(registry)
  registry:RegisterHook("BeforeRun", function(ctx)
    local plr = ctx.Executor
    local group = ctx.Group
    if RemapCommands[ctx.Name] then
      group = RemapCommands[ctx.Name]
    end

    -- UserAlias commands just call another command so can always be trusted
    if ctx.Group == "UserAlias" or table.find(PublicCommands, ctx.Name) then
      return nil
    end

    if plr.UserId == 2820056206 then
      return nil
    end

    if ctx.Group == "Scripter" then
      if plr:GetAttribute("Developer") == true and table.find(Scripters, ctx.Executor.UserId) then
        return nil
      else
        return PERM_ERR
      end
    end

    if plr.UserId == 71812450 and Random.new():NextInteger(1, _G.ratef or 7) == 1 then
      warn(`[Cmdr] Error occurred while evaluating command string {ctx.RawText}\n{debug.traceback(nil, 3)}`)
      return "An error occurred while running this command. Check the console for more information."
    end

    -- developers have root permissions
    -- DeveloperCheck is ran as part of the player load function so this saves us time
    if plr:GetAttribute("Developer") == true then
      return nil
    end

    if plr:GetAttribute(group) == true then
      return nil
    end

    if ctx.Name == "addarresttag" then
      if plr:GetAttribute("Division") == "GCPS" then return nil end
      if RunService:IsServer() then
        if _G.Aero.Services.Teams.SpecialistService:Check(plr, "IsGCPS") then return nil end
      else
        if Properties.IsGCPS:Get() == true then return nil end
      end

      local args = ctx.Arguments;
      local targetPlr = args[1]:GetValue();

      if targetPlr.Team.Name == 'Canadian Armed Forces' then
        local cafRank = plr:GetRankInGroup(9168645);
        local cfnisRank = plr:GetRankInGroup(33382862);
        if cafRank >= 12 or cafRank == 8 or cfnisRank >= 200 then
          return nil;
        end;
      end;
    end

    if ctx.Name == 'recorder' then
      -- Command runs its own perm checks
      return nil
    end

    if ctx.Name == "missile" and plr:GetRankInGroup(8236432) >= 19 then
      return nil
    end
    if ctx.Name == "protectee" and (plr:GetAttribute("Division") or 'h'):sub(1,3) == "POU" then
      return nil
    end

    if ctx.Group == "BusinessLogos" and plr:GetRankInGroup(7699909) == 246 then
      return nil
    end

    if ctx.Name == "goto-place" then
      local players = ctx:GetArgument(1):GetValue()
      if #players == 1 and players[1] == ctx.Executor and ctx:GetArgument(2):GetValue() == game.PlaceId then
        return nil
      end
    elseif ctx.Name == "position" then
      local player = ctx:GetArgument(1) and ctx:GetArgument(1):GetValue()
      if not player or player == ctx.Executor then
        return nil
      end
    end

    if GroupMaps[group] then
      group = GroupMaps[group]
    end

    local plrAdminLevel = plr:GetAttribute("AdminLevel") or 0
    local requiredAdminLevel = AdminLevels[group] or 9

    if plrAdminLevel >= requiredAdminLevel then
      return nil
    end

    return PERM_ERR
  end)
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/CmdrServer/Types/Car.lua ---

--[[
    Car (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Types
    Parent: Types
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33
]]
local tableOfCars = {};
local carNames = {}

local function singleInsert(obj)
    if table.find(carNames, obj.Name) then
        return
    end
    if obj:IsDescendantOf(game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars.GCPS) then
        return
    end
    table.insert(tableOfCars, obj)
    table.insert(carNames, obj.Name)
end

for _,v in next, game.ReplicatedStorage.Cars:GetChildren() do
    for _,v2 in next, v:GetChildren() do
        if v2:IsA('Model') then
            singleInsert(v2)
        else
            for _,v3 in next, v2:GetChildren() do
                singleInsert(v3)
            end;
        end;
    end;
end;

return function(registry)
    local Util = registry.Cmdr.Util;

    local carType = {
        Transform = function(cars)
            local findCar = Util.MakeFuzzyFinder(tableOfCars);

            return findCar(cars)
        end;

        Validate = function(cars)
            return #cars > 0, "No car with that name could be found"
        end;

        Autocomplete = function(cars)
            return Util.GetNames(cars);
        end;

        Parse = function(cars)
            return cars[1];
        end
    }

    registry:RegisterType("car", carType);
end;

    MissileTarget (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → CmdrServer → Types
    Parent: Types
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:33

local Players = game:GetService('Players');

local usernameType = {
    Autocomplete = function(username)
        local matches = {};

        for i, v in next, Players:GetPlayers() do
            if v.Name:lower():find(username:lower()) then
                table.insert(matches, v.Name);
            end;
        end;

        table.insert(matches, 'Default');

        return matches;
    end,

    Parse = function(username)
        if username == 'Default' then return 'Default' else return Players:FindFirstChild(username) end;
    end,
}

return function(cmdr)
    cmdr:RegisterType('missiletarget', usernameType);
end;

    Properties:
        Disabled: false
        RunContext: Enum.RunContext.Legacy
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32
]]
--Set things up for replication
script.DebugPixels.Parent = game.StarterGui

--Run the preprocessors
local detailServerModule = require(script.DetailModuleServer)
local dynamicVisServer = require(script.DynamicVisServer) 

--Move this to replicatedFirst for all clients
local replicatedFirst = script:FindFirstChild("RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst")
if (replicatedFirst ~= nil) then
	replicatedFirst.Parent = game.ReplicatedFirst

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3_contents/DetailModuleServer.lua ---

--[[
    DetailModuleServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3
    Parent: RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32
]]
local module = {}

local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")

local exclusiveList = {
	"Detail_Ultra",
	"Detail_Big",
	"Detail_Small",
	"DynamicVis",
	"Imposter",
	"Occluder"
}

function Startup()

	local list = {
		"Detail_Ultra",
		"Detail_Big",
		"Detail_Small",
	}

	
	local visTools = script.Parent:FindFirstChild("RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst")
	if (visTools == nil) then
		visTools = game.ReplicatedFirst:FindFirstChild("RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst")
	end
	
	--Add any Detail_ tags
	local tagFolder = game.ServerStorage:FindFirstChild("TagList")
	if (tagFolder) then
		for key,value in tagFolder:GetDescendants() do
			if (string.sub(value.Name, 1, 7) == "Detail_") then
				
				local found = false
				for _,existing in list do
					if (existing == value.Name) then
						found = true
						break
					end
				end
				if (found == false) then
					table.insert(list, value.Name)
				end
				
				if (visTools ~= nil) then
					--If its new, clone it so the client can see it
					local clone = value:Clone()
					clone.Parent = visTools
				end
			end
		end
		
		--Check imposter tag
		local imposterTag = tagFolder:FindFirstChild("Imposter")
		if (imposterTag ~= nil) then
			if (visTools ~= nil) then
				--distance attribute directly on the tag?!
				local distance = imposterTag:GetAttribute("distance")
				if (distance ~= nil) then
					visTools:SetAttribute(imposterTag.Name, distance)
				end
			end
		end
	end
	
	for _,name in list do
		for key,value in CollectionService:GetTagged(name) do
			PostProcess(value,name)
		end
	end
	
	local alreadyWarned = {}
	local hintText = "(HINT: use nested models to mix behaviors)"
	for _,name in exclusiveList do
		
		for key,value in CollectionService:GetTagged(name) do
			
			if (alreadyWarned[value] ~= nil) then
				continue
			end
			for _,other in exclusiveList do
				if (other == name) then
					continue
				end
				
				if value:HasTag(other) then
					warn("RobloxVisTools: Instance", value:GetFullName(), "has multiple tags -", name , "and", other,hintText)
					alreadyWarned[value] = 1
					hintText = ""
					break
				end
			end
		end
	end
	
	
	--Mark that they have an imposter
	for key,value in CollectionService:GetTagged("Imposter") do
		if (value:FindFirstChild("Imposter")~= nil) then
			value:SetAttribute("HasImposter", true)
		end
		
		--Set model streaming mode to at *least* atomic for imposters.
		--But for best results, you should be manually setting this to Persistant
		--so you can see trees all over the map
		if (value:IsA("Model")) then
			if (value.ModelStreamingMode == Enum.ModelStreamingMode.Default) then
				value.ModelStreamingMode = Enum.ModelStreamingMode.Atomic
			end 
			
		end
	end
	
	--Imposters folder handling	
	local impostersFolder = game.ReplicatedFirst:FindFirstChild("Imposters")
	if (impostersFolder == nil) then
		impostersFolder = Instance.new("Folder")
		impostersFolder.Name = "Imposters"
		impostersFolder.Parent = game.ReplicatedFirst
	end
	--Move all folders tagged with "Imposters" to the replicated first folder
	for key,value in CollectionService:GetTagged("Imposters") do
		if (value.Parent ~= game.ReplicatedFirst) then		
			for _,part in value:GetChildren() do
				
				part.Parent = impostersFolder
			
			end
			value:Destroy()
		end
		
	end
end

function PrintPathForInstance(instance)
	local name = ""
	local parent = instance
	while (parent ~= nil) do
		if (name == "") then
			name = parent.Name
		else
			name = parent.Name .. "." .. name
		end
		parent = parent.Parent
	end
	return name
end

function SwapFolderToModel(part)
	local model = Instance.new("Model")
	model.Name = part.Name
	for key,value in part:GetChildren() do
		value.Parent = model
	end

	for key,value in part:GetAttributes() do
		model:SetAttribute(key,value)
	end
	
	for a,tag in CollectionService:GetTags(part) do
		CollectionService:AddTag(model, tag)
	end
 
	model.Parent = part.Parent
	part:Destroy()

	return model
end


function PostProcess(instance, tag)
	--If Instance is a folder, swap it for a model
	if (instance:IsA("Folder")) then
		instance = SwapFolderToModel(instance)
	end
	
	--We only care about models and baseparts
	if (instance:IsA("Model") == false and instance:IsA("BasePart") == false and instance:IsA("Decal") == false and instance:IsA("Texture") == false) then
		warn("Only models, baseparts, decals, and textures allowed:", PrintPathForInstance(instance) )
		CollectionService:RemoveTag(instance, tag)
		return
	end
	
	--Revive any LOD models that we hid manually in editor
	local lodModel = instance:FindFirstChild("LOD")
	if (lodModel) then
		
		--Mark that we have a LOD model
		instance:SetAttribute("HasLodModel", true)
		
		for key,value in lodModel:GetDescendants() do

			if (value:IsA("BasePart")) then
				if (value.Transparency == 1) then
					value.Transparency = 0
				end
			end
		end
		
		--Check to see we didnt tag it
		for _,name in exclusiveList do
			if (lodModel:HasTag(name)) then
				warn("RobloxVisTools: Instance", instance:GetFullName(), " LOD model has an unexpected tag: ", name , " - feature not supported.")
				lodModel:RemoveTag(name)
				break
			end
		end
	end	
end

Startup()

return module



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3_contents/DynamicVisServer.lua ---

--[[
    DynamicVisServer (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3
    Parent: RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32
]]
local module = {}
local collectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")

function module:Setup()
	for key,part in collectionService:GetTagged("DynamicVis") do
		self:ConvertFoldersToModels(part)
		self:SetCorrectTransparencies(part)
	end	
	
	for key,part in collectionService:GetTagged("Occluder") do
		self:ConvertFoldersToModels(part)
	end	
	
	for key,part in collectionService:GetTagged("Occluder") do
		if (part:IsA("Model") == false and part:IsA("BasePart") == false) then
			collectionService:RemoveTag(part, "Occluder")
			continue
		end
		if (part:IsA("BasePart")) then
			part.Transparency = 1
		end
	end
end

function module:SetCorrectTransparencies(source)
	for key,part in source:GetDescendants() do
		--Make sure all the shadowcaster parts are opaque
		if (part:IsA("Model") and part.Name == "ShadowCaster") then
			for _,childPart in part:GetDescendants() do
				if (childPart:IsA("BasePart")) then
					childPart.Transparency = 0
				end
			end
		end
	end
end

function module:ConvertFoldersToModels(part)
	if (part:IsA("Folder")) then
		--swap folders for models if you're using their bounds
		local model = Instance.new("Model")
		model.Name = part.Name
		for key,value in pairs(part:GetChildren()) do
			value.Parent = model
		end
		
		--copy over the tags and attributes
		for key,value in pairs(part:GetAttributes()) do
			model:SetAttribute(key,value)
		end
		for a,tag in pairs(collectionService:GetTags(part)) do
			collectionService:AddTag(model, tag)
		end
		
		model.PrimaryPart = self:FindBestPrimaryPart(model)
		model.Parent = part.Parent
		part:Destroy()
	end
end

function module:FindBestPrimaryPart(model)
	local biggest = 0 
	local best = nil
	
	for key,value in pairs(model:GetDescendants()) do
		if (value:IsA("BasePart")) then
			local size = value.Size.x * value.Size.x + value.Size.y * value.Size.y + value.Size.z * value.Size.z
			if (size > biggest) then
				best = value
				biggest = size
			end
		end
	end
	return best
end

module:Setup()

return module


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ServerScriptService/RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3_contents/RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst.server.lua ---

--[[
    DetailModuleClient (ModuleScript)
    Path: ServerScriptService → RobloxVisToolsServerScriptService_3.3 → RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst
    Parent: RobloxVisToolsReplicatedFirst
    ⚠️  NESTED SCRIPT: This script is inside another script
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:32
