local CollectionService = game:GetService("CollectionService")

local module = {}

--assets
module.quads = script.Parent:FindFirstChild("Quads")

--Settings
module.allowDebug = script.Parent:GetAttribute("allowDebugInLive") or (game.ReplicatedFirst:FindFirstChild("allowDebugInLive")~=nil)

--Always allow it in studio
if (game["Run Service"]:IsStudio() == true) then
	module.allowDebug = true
end

module.debugging = false and module.allowDebug
module.drawDebugText = script.parent:GetAttribute("enableDebugOnStart") and module.allowDebug
module.override = false

--General objects, the biggest one of these thats on the grid affects performance a little bit, as it determines the grid size
module.tagList = {	{name = "Detail_Ultra",	distance = 800, useGrid = false},
					{name = "Detail_Big", 	distance = 400, useGrid = true},
    				{name = "Detail_Small",	distance = 200, useGrid = true}}

--Imposter range - note 600 seems to be about the right distance for imposters with baked shadows (roblox stops shadows after this)
module.imposterDistance = script.Parent:GetAttribute("Imposter") or 350
module.imposterMaxDistance = script.Parent:GetAttribute("ImposterMax") or 2000  

--Distance the camera has to move to be considered a teleport
module.teleportSize = script.Parent:GetAttribute("TeleportSize") or 40

--Folder to go find imposter surfaces
module.folder = game.ReplicatedFirst:FindFirstChild("Imposters")

--Check when the camera has moved ~x units
module.stepSize = 20
module.debugGui = nil
module.animSpeed = 2
module.imposterAnimSpeed = 2 --multiplier
module.imposterMsBudget = 2 --2ms
module.imposterUpdates=0
module.impostersUpdating = false
module.imposterVerticalAngleTolerance = 0.75 --higher = steeper angle required. Imposter will turn back into a tree if you get above it eg: helicopter
module.supressAnimationFrames = 0
module.largestGridDistance = 0


--Internals
module.records = {}
module.ultraRecords = {}
module.movingRecords = {}
module.debugSupression = false

module.detailMsBudget = 4 --4ms
module.lastGrid = nil
module.processing = false --coroutine for details already running
module.detailsDirty = false 	   --trigger coroutine for details
module.setup = false
module.animating = {}
module.animatingLights = {}
module.debugTris = {}

module.grid = {}
module.oldSet = {} --What we processed last "step"
module.gridSize = Vector3.new(400,2000,400)

module.newlyVisibleRecords = {}	--Records that have been freshly set up this frame
module.imposters = {}

--debugging
module.recordCount = 0
module.visibleDetails = 0
module.visibleMovingDetails = 0
module.visibleImposterModels = 0
module.visibleImposterQuads = 0
module.detailsAnimating = 0
module.tooMuchStuffAnimating = 200
module.markParts = false


--Call this to process the configuration again on detail objects
function module:ForceUpdateAllTags()
		
	local cameraPos = game.workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position
	
	--Loop through all of the current world objects...
	for key,record in self.records do
		task.spawn(function()
			while(record.loaded ~= true) do
				wait()
			end
			local instance = record.instance
			
			self:ConfigureRecordDistance(instance, record, record.tag.useGrid, record.tag.moves, record.tag.distance)
			self:UpdateVis(record, cameraPos)	
		end)
	end
end




--Call this to prevent animation for the next X frames
function module:SupressAnimations(numFrames : number)
	module.supressAnimationFrames = numFrames
end

function module:AnimateRecord(record, speed)
	
	if (record.animate ~= true or module.supressAnimationFrames > 0) then
		self:SnapAnimateRecord(record, speed)
		return
	end
	
	--If too much stuff is blending in, go hyperfast
	if (self.detailsAnimating > self.tooMuchStuffAnimating) then
		speed *= 4
	end
 	
	if (record.lodModel == nil) then
		self:AnimatePart(record.instance, record.instance, speed, 0, record.reparent)
		for key,part in record.instance:GetDescendants() do
			self:AnimatePart(record.instance, part, speed, 0, record.reparent)
		end
	else
		--we have a lod model		
		local lodDelay = 0
		local detailDelay = 1
		if (speed < 0) then
			lodDelay = 1
			detailDelay = 0
		end
		
		record.lodModel.Parent = record.parent
		self:AnimatePart(record.lodModel, record.lodModel, -speed * 2, lodDelay, true) --LOD models ALWAYS deparent
		for key,part in record.lodModel:GetDescendants() do
			self:AnimatePart(record.lodModel, part, -speed * 2, lodDelay, true)
		end
		
		--regular parts
		self:AnimatePart(record.instance, record.instance, speed * 2,detailDelay, record.reparent)
		for key,part in record.instance:GetDescendants() do
			self:AnimatePart(record.instance, part, speed * 2, detailDelay, record.reparent)
		end
	end
end

function module:SnapRecordToTransparent(record)
	
	local function SetFullyTransparent(part)

		if (part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture") ) then
			part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 1
		elseif part:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
			part.Enabled = false
		end  

		if (part:IsA("Light")) then
			local sourceBrightness = part:GetAttribute("Brightness") 
			if (sourceBrightness == nil) then
				part:SetAttribute("Brightness", part.Brightness)
			end
			part.Brightness =0
		end	
	end
	
	--regular parts
	SetFullyTransparent(record.instance)
	for key,part in record.instance:GetDescendants() do
		SetFullyTransparent(part)
	end
	

end

function module:SnapAnimateRecord(record, speed)
	
	--Clear out any animations
	self:ClearAnimations(record)
	
	if (record.lodModel ~= nil) then
		if (speed > 0) then
	
			--Make LOD visible, model invisible
			if (record.reparent == true) then
				record.instance.Parent = nil
			else
				--Make transparent 
				self:SnapRecordToTransparent(record)
			end
			
			--Make the LOD Visible!
			record.lodModel.Parent = record.parent
		else
			
			--Make LOD invisible, model visible
			record.lodModel.Parent = nil
			
			if (record.reparent == true) then
				--Let the collection service know why 
				record.parentReason = "AnimatingSnap"
				record.instance.Parent = record.parent
			end
			
		end
	else
		if (speed > 0) then
			--Make Invisible!			
			
			if (record.reparent == true) then
				record.instance.Parent = nil	
			else
				--Make transparent 
				self:SnapRecordToTransparent(record)
			end
			
		else
			--Make visible! 
			--Doesn't need to do anything because we just cleared its animation
			
			--Let the collection service know why
			if (record.reparent == true) then
				record.parentReason = "AnimatingSnap"
				record.instance.Parent = record.parent
			end
		end
	end
end

function module:ClearAnimations(record)
	
	--Dont need to animate it if we're just going to reparent it
	if (record.animate == false and record.reparent == true) then
		return
	end

	--LodModels
	if (record.lodModel ~= nil) then	
		module:ClearAnimation(record.lodModel)
		for key,part in record.lodModel:GetDescendants() do
			self:ClearAnimation(part)
		end
	end

	--regular parts
	self:ClearAnimation(record.instance)
	for key,part in record.instance:GetDescendants() do
		self:ClearAnimation(part)
	end
end

--Resets an object to full visibility
function module:ClearAnimation(part)
	if (part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture") ) then
		part.LocalTransparencyModifier = 0
		local record = self.animating[part]
		self.animating[part] = nil
	elseif part:IsA("SurfaceGui") then
		--Well, this wont work if you manually disbled the surfaceGui, todo?
		part.Enabled = true	
	end  
	
	if (part:IsA("Light")) then
		local sourceBrightness = part:GetAttribute("Brightness") 
		if (sourceBrightness ~= nil) then
			part.Brightness = sourceBrightness
		end
		
		self.animatingLights[part] = nil 
	end	
end

function module:AnimatePart(parentInstance, part, speed, delayTime, reparent)
	--Stuff with LocalTransparencyModifier
	if (part:IsA("BasePart") or part:IsA("Decal") or part:IsA("Texture")) then
		local partRecord = {}
		partRecord.part = part
		partRecord.delayTime = delayTime * 0.5
		
		if (speed < 0) then
			--Fading in, start with transparency of 1, go to 0
			partRecord.transparency = 1
			partRecord.dir = speed
		else
			--Fading out, transparency of 0, go to 1
			partRecord.transparency = 0
			partRecord.dir = speed
		end

		--If we were already animating, grab whatever the alpha was so we don't pop
		local prevRecord = self.animating[part] 
		if (prevRecord ~= nil) then
			partRecord.transparency = prevRecord.transparency
		end

		partRecord.parentInstance = parentInstance
		partRecord.reparent = reparent
		
		part.LocalTransparencyModifier = partRecord.transparency
		self.animating[part] = partRecord
		
		return
			
	elseif (part:IsA("SurfaceGui")) then
		
		--We cant fade these, so just enable/disable them
		if (speed < 0) then
			part.Enabled = true
		else
			part.Enabled = false
		end
		
		return
	end
	
	if (part:IsA("Light")) then

		local sourceBrightness = part:GetAttribute("Brightness") 
		if (sourceBrightness == nil) then
			sourceBrightness = part.Brightness
			part:SetAttribute("Brightness", sourceBrightness)
		end

		local partRecord = {}
		partRecord.delayTime = delayTime  
		partRecord.part = part
		partRecord.brightness = sourceBrightness
		partRecord.reparent = reparent

		if (speed < 0) then
			--Fading in, start with transparency of 1, go to 0
			partRecord.transparency = 1
			partRecord.dir = speed
		else
			--Fading out, transparency of 0, go to 1
			partRecord.transparency = 0
			partRecord.dir = speed
		end

		--If we were already animating, grab whatever the alpha was so we don't pop
		local prevRecord = self.animatingLights[part] 
		if (prevRecord~=nil) then
			partRecord.transparency = prevRecord.transparency
		end

		partRecord.parentInstance = parentInstance
		part.Brightness = partRecord.brightness * (1-partRecord.transparency)
		self.animatingLights[part] = partRecord
		
		return
	end
end

function module:AddToGrid(record)
	local grid = self.grid[record.key]
	if grid==nil then
		grid = {}
		self.grid[record.key] = grid
	end
	grid[record.instance] = record
end

function module:RemoveFromGrid(record)
	local grid = self.grid[record.key]
	if (grid) then
		grid[record.instance] = nil
	end
end
 
function module:UpdateVis(record, cameraPos)
	if (record.parent == nil) then
		return
	end
	
	--see if we're in the scene
	local position = self:GetPosition(record)
	local dist = (position - cameraPos).magnitude
 	
	if (self.debugSupression == true) then
		dist = 0
	end
  
	if (dist > record.distance) then
		--Can see it
		if(record.visible == true) then
			if (self.debugging == true) then
				print("Detail hiding", record.instance.Name)
			end
	 
			record.visible = false
			
			if (record.lodModel) then
				record.lodModel.Parent = record.parent
			end
			
			--record.instance.Parent = nil -- Dont deparent yet, gotta fade
			self:AnimateRecord(record, 1) --Fade out
		end
	else
		--can't see it
		if (record.visible == false) then
			if (self.debugging == true) then
				print("Detail showing", record.instance.Name)
			end
	 
			record.visible = true
		 
			--Parent it to the world, but make sure the collection service also knows why
			if (record.reparent == true) then
				record.parentReason = "Animating"
				record.instance.Parent = record.parent
			end
			
			self:AnimateRecord(record,-1) --Fade in
		end		
	end
end

function module:PrintPathForInstance(instance)
	local name = ""
	local parent = instance
	while (parent ~= nil) do
		if (name == "") then
			name = parent.Name
		else
			name = parent.Name .. "." .. name
		end
		parent = parent.Parent
	end
	return name
end

function module:CalculateKey(worldPos)
	return Vector3.new(math.floor(worldPos.x/self.gridSize.x),math.floor(worldPos.y/self.gridSize.y), math.floor(worldPos.z/self.gridSize.z))
end

function module:GetPosition(record)
	
	if (record.isDecalOrTexture) then
		return record.parent.Position 
	end
	
	if (record.isModel) then
		if (record.instance.PrimaryPart ~= nil) then
			return record.instance.PrimaryPart.Position
		end
		return record.instance:GetModelCFrame().Position
	end
	return record.instance.Position
end

function module:CalculateRadius(instance)
	local sizeVec 
	if (instance:IsA("Decal") or instance:IsA("Texture")) then
		sizeVec = instance.Parent.Size
	elseif instance:IsA("BasePart") then
		sizeVec =instance.Size
	else
		local cf, size = instance:GetBoundingBox()
		sizeVec = size
	end
	
	return (math.max(math.max(sizeVec.x, sizeVec.y), sizeVec.z)) / 2
end


function module:ConfigureRecordDistance(instance, record, useGrid, moves, dist)
	
	record.useGrid = useGrid
	record.moves = moves
	
	local distanceAttribute = instance:GetAttribute("distance")
	if (distanceAttribute ~= nil) then
		dist = distanceAttribute
	end

	record.distance = dist + self:CalculateRadius(record.instance)

	--Cap the distance to the max sized specified (grid optimisation)
	if (useGrid) then
		if (record.distance > self.largestGridDistance) then
			record.distance = self.largestGridDistance
		end
	end

end
-- This triggers on every parenting
function module:OnDetailAdded(instance, dist, useGrid, moves, animated, reparent, tag)
	--If we already know its new, skip this
	if (self.newlyVisibleRecords[instance] ~= nil) then
		return
	end
	
	--if this already exists in our records, tap it as a new record and exit
	local existingRecord = self.records[instance]
	if (existingRecord ~= nil) then
		
		--If this is parented without a parentReason, then this object was parented by an external system like streaming
		if (existingRecord.parentReason == nil) then
			--print("Newly visible ", instance.Name)
			self.newlyVisibleRecords[instance] = self.records[instance] 
		end
		existingRecord.parentReason = nil
		return
	end
		
	--We only care about models and baseparts
	if (instance:IsA("Model") == false and instance:IsA("BasePart") == false and instance:IsA("Decal") == false and instance:IsA("Texture") == false) then
		warn("Only models, baseparts, decals, and textures allowed: ", self:PrintPathForInstance(instance) )
		return
	end
	
	local thread
	thread = task.spawn(function()

		--Good to go
		if (self.debugging == true) then
			print("Detail Adding ",instance.Name, " moves:", moves)
		end
			 
		--Time to set up a record to watch the instance
		local record = {}
		
		record.tag = tag
		record.instance = instance
		record.visible = true
		record.animate = animated
		record.reparent = reparent
		record.loaded = false
		record.useGrid = useGrid
		record.moves = moves
		
		self:ConfigureRecordDistance(instance, record, useGrid, moves, dist)
		
		self.records[instance] = record
		
		--If its not in the workspace, wait for a parental change (eg: replicated first)
		if (game.Workspace:IsAncestorOf(instance) == false) then

			local loop = true
			local connection = instance.AncestryChanged:Connect(function(child, parent)
				if (game.Workspace:IsAncestorOf(instance) == true) then
					coroutine.resume(thread)
				end
			end)
			
			coroutine.yield(thread)
			--we've been resumed!			
			connection:Disconnect()
		end
		
		--If we have a lod model, we have to wait for it to replicate before we can continue
		local hasLodModel = instance:GetAttribute("HasLodModel")
		if (hasLodModel ~= nil and hasLodModel == true) then
			--Wait for LOD model replication
			while(true) do
				local lodModel = instance:FindFirstChild("LOD") 
				if (lodModel) then
					lodModel.Parent = nil
					record.lodModel = lodModel
					break
				else
					wait()
				end
			end
		end
		
		local animateValue = instance:GetAttribute("animate")
		if (animateValue ~= nil) then
			record.animate = animateValue
		end
		
		--Cache how we're going to get its position	
		record.isDecalOrTexture = false
		record.isModel = false
		
		if (instance:IsA("Decal") or instance:IsA("Texture")) then
			record.isDecalOrTexture = true
		elseif (instance:IsA("Model")) then
			record.isModel = true
		end
		
		if (self.markParts == true) then
			local bounds = Instance.new("SelectionBox")
			bounds.Adornee = instance
			bounds.Parent = instance
			bounds.Color3 = Color3.new(0.3,1,0.3)
			bounds.SurfaceColor3 = Color3.new(0.3,1,0.3)
			bounds.SurfaceTransparency = 0.85
		end

		--Do some work to figure out the intended parent when we're in the scene
		--easy check - Do we have a parent right now?
		if (game.Workspace:IsAncestorOf(record.instance) == true) then
			record.parent = instance.Parent
		end

		--Slightly less easy check - watch for ancestory changed and check again (eg: we got parented to game.lighting)
		instance.AncestryChanged:Connect(function(child, parent)
			--Do we have a parent?
			if (game.Workspace:IsAncestorOf(record.instance) == true) then
				record.parent = instance.Parent
			end
		end)
				
		--Add a dummy connection to a property of instance, so we can tell when the instance gets Destroyed()
		record.instanceSignal = record.instance:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Name"):Connect(function() end)
		record.instance.Destroying:Connect(function()
			record.instanceSignal:Disconnect()
			record.instanceSignal = nil
		end)
		
		--Ultra objects dont go in the grid, but smaller objects do
		if (record.useGrid == true) then
			
			--Add them to the grid	
			record.key = self:CalculateKey(self:GetPosition(record))
			self:AddToGrid(record)
			
			--Add them to the old set
			self.oldSet[record.instance] = record

			if (record.isModel == false) then
				local partToTrack = record.instance
				
				if (record.isDecalOrTexture) then
					partToTrack = record.instance.Parent
				end
				
				--Todo: this doesnt work				
				--Move grid if the part moved
				record.transformChanged = partToTrack:GetPropertyChangedSignal("Position"):Connect(function() 
					local newKey = self:CalculateKey(self:GetPosition(record))
					if (newKey ~= record.key) then
						self:RemoveFromGrid(record)
						record.key = newKey
						self:AddToGrid(record)
					end
				end)
			else
				--Move grid if the model moved
				record.transformChanged = record.instance:GetPropertyChangedSignal("WorldPivot"):Connect(function() 
					local newKey = self:CalculateKey(self:GetPosition(record))
					if (newKey ~= record.key) then
						self:RemoveFromGrid(record)
						record.key = newKey
						self:AddToGrid(record)
					end

				end)
			end
		else
			if (record.moves == true) then
				self.movingRecords[instance] = record				
			else
				self.ultraRecords[instance] = record	
			end
			
		end
		
		--Tag it as a new record, which will set its initial state based on distance
		self.newlyVisibleRecords[instance] = record
		
		record.loaded = true
		self.recordCount +=1
	end)
end

function module:ConfigureTags()

	for _,value in script.Parent:GetChildren() do
		local name = value.Name
		if (string.sub(name, 1, 7) == "Detail_") then
			local newRecord = nil

			for _,record in self.tagList do
				if (record.name == name) then
					newRecord = record
					break
				end
			end
			if (newRecord == nil) then

				newRecord = {}
				newRecord.moves = false
				newRecord.useGrid = true
				newRecord.name = name
				newRecord.distance = 50

				if (self.debugging == true) then
					print("New Detail tag registered:", name , " distance:", newRecord.distance, " moves:", newRecord.moves)
				end
				table.insert(self.tagList, newRecord)
			end

			newRecord.reparent = true
			newRecord.animate = true
			newRecord.moves = false			

			if (value:GetAttribute("distance") ~= nil) then
				newRecord.distance = value:GetAttribute("distance")
			end

			if (value:GetAttribute("usegrid") == false) then
				newRecord.useGrid = false
			end

			if (value:GetAttribute("animate") == false) then
				newRecord.animate = false
			end

			if (value:GetAttribute("deparent") == false) then
				newRecord.reparent = false
			end

			if (value:GetAttribute("moves") == true) then
				newRecord.useGrid = false
				newRecord.moves = true
				newRecord.reparent = false
			end		
						
			newRecord.configurationDistance = newRecord.distance
		end
	end

	--Setup the known ones from self.tagList
	self.largestGridDistance = 0
	for key,record in self.tagList do

		--Grab the largest one
		if (record.useGrid == true and record.distance > self.largestGridDistance) then
			self.largestGridDistance = record.distance
		end		
	end
end

function module:Setup()
	if (self.setup == true) then
		return
	end
	self.setup = true
	
	self:ConfigureTags()
	
	--Start everything
	for key,record in self.tagList do
		
		for key,instance in CollectionService:GetTagged(record.name) do
			module:OnDetailAdded(instance, record.distance, record.useGrid, record.moves, record.animate, record.reparent, record)
		end
		
		CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal(record.name):Connect(function(instance)
			module:OnDetailAdded(instance, record.distance, record.useGrid, record.moves, record.animate, record.reparent, record)
		end)	
	end
 
	for key,instance in CollectionService:GetTagged("Imposter") do
		self:ImposterSetup(instance)
	end
	CollectionService:GetInstanceAddedSignal("Imposter"):Connect(function(instance)
		self:ImposterSetup(instance)
	end)
	
	self.cameraPreviousCFrame = game.workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame
end

function module:DrawUIText(pos, textData, color, size)
	local text = Instance.new("TextLabel")
	text.AutoLocalize = false
	text.Text = textData
	text.BackgroundTransparency = 1
	text.TextSize = size
	text.TextColor3 = color
	text.Position = UDim2.new(0,pos.x, 0, pos.y)
	text.TextXAlignment = Enum.TextXAlignment.Left
	text.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Bottom	
	text.Parent = self.debugGui

	table.insert(self.debugTris, text)
	return text	
end

function module:ProcessDetailObject(record, cameraPos)
	if (record.loaded == false) then
		return
	end
	
	--Did we get destroyed since last time?
	if (record.instanceSignal == nil or record.instanceSignal.Connected == false) then
		if (self.debugging == true) then
			print("Detail destroyed", record.instance.Name)

		end
		if (record.instance ~= nil) then
			self:RemoveFromGrid(record)
			self.records[record.instance] = nil
			self.ultraRecords[record.instance] = nil
			self.movingRecords[record.instance] = nil
		end
		self.recordCount -=1
		return
	end

	--Update 
	self:UpdateVis(record, cameraPos)
	if (record.visible) then
		if (record.moves) then
			self.visibleMovingDetails += 1	
		else
			self.visibleDetails += 1
		end
	end
end

function module:UpdateAnimations(dt)
	
	debug.profilebegin("Update Animations")
	
	--Fades for things with local transparencies
	self.detailsAnimating = 0
	for key,partRecord in self.animating do
		self.detailsAnimating += 1

		if (partRecord.delayTime > 0) then
			partRecord.delayTime -= dt * self.animSpeed
		else

			partRecord.transparency += partRecord.dir * dt * self.animSpeed

			--Animation finished, fully opqaue
			if (partRecord.transparency < 0) then
				partRecord.transparency = 0
				self.animating[partRecord.part] = nil	
			end

			--Animation finished, fully transparent now
			if (partRecord.transparency > 1) then
				partRecord.transparency = 1
				self.animating[partRecord.part] = nil

				--Remove the whole object from the world
				if (partRecord.reparent) then
					partRecord.parentInstance.Parent = nil	
				end
			end
		end
		partRecord.part.LocalTransparencyModifier = partRecord.transparency
	end

	--Fades for lights
	for key,partRecord in self.animatingLights do
		self.detailsAnimating += 1
		if (partRecord.delayTime > 0) then
			partRecord.delayTime -= dt * self.animSpeed
		else
			partRecord.transparency += partRecord.dir * dt* self.animSpeed
			if (partRecord.transparency <0) then
				partRecord.transparency = 0
				self.animatingLights[partRecord.part] = nil	
			end
			if (partRecord.transparency > 1) then
				partRecord.transparency =1
				self.animatingLights[partRecord.part] = nil

				--Remove the whole object from the world
				if (partRecord.reparent == true) then
					partRecord.parentInstance.Parent = nil					
				end

			end
		end
		partRecord.part.Brightness = partRecord.brightness * (1 - partRecord.transparency)
	end
	debug.profileend()
end

function module:UpdateDetails(cameraPos, dt)
	if (self.detailsDirty == false) then
		return
	end
		
	if (self.processing == true) then
		return
	end	

	self.detailsDirty = false
	self.processing = true
	
	local nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.detailMsBudget) 
	task.spawn(function()
		debug.profilebegin("Update Details")
		
		self.visibleDetails = 0

		local cellRadiusX = math.ceil(self.largestGridDistance / self.gridSize.x) 
		local cellRadiusY = math.ceil(self.largestGridDistance / self.gridSize.y)
		local cellRadiusZ = math.ceil(self.largestGridDistance / self.gridSize.z)

		local minx = math.floor(cameraPos.x / self.gridSize.x) - cellRadiusX
		local miny = math.floor(cameraPos.y / self.gridSize.y) - cellRadiusY
		local minz = math.floor(cameraPos.z / self.gridSize.z) - cellRadiusZ
		local maxx = math.floor(cameraPos.x / self.gridSize.x) + cellRadiusX  
		local maxy = math.floor(cameraPos.y / self.gridSize.y) + cellRadiusY  
		local maxz = math.floor(cameraPos.z / self.gridSize.z) + cellRadiusZ  

		local newSet = {}
		local count = 0
		
		debug.profilebegin("Update Grid")
		for x=minx, maxx do
			for y = miny, maxy do
				for z = minz, maxz do

					local grid = self.grid[Vector3.new(x,y,z)]
					if (grid) then
						for key,record in grid do

							--Calculate a shiny new set
							newSet[record.instance] = record
							--Merge in with the old set
							self.oldSet[record.instance] = record
						end
					end
				end
			end
		end
		debug.profileend()

		--Check the vis
		local counter = 0
		for instance,record in self.oldSet do
			self:ProcessDetailObject(record, cameraPos)
			
			--Cap at 2ms per frame
			counter+=1
			if (counter > 100) then
				counter = 0
				if (tick() > nextPause) then
				 
					debug.profileend()
					task.wait()
					debug.profilebegin("Update Details")
					nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.detailMsBudget) 
				end
			end
		end

		self.oldSet = newSet
		self.processing = false
		
		counter = 0
		for instance,record in self.ultraRecords do
			self:ProcessDetailObject(record, cameraPos)

			--Cap at 2ms per frame
			counter+=1
			if (counter > 100) then
				counter = 0
				if (tick() > nextPause) then

					debug.profileend()
					task.wait()
					debug.profilebegin("Update Details")
					nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.detailMsBudget) 
				end
			end
		end
		
		debug.profileend()
	end)
end

function module:UpdateMovingDetails(cameraPos, dt)
	--Check the vis for moving records
	
	task.spawn(function()

		debug.profilebegin("Update Moving Details")
		self.visibleMovingDetails = 0

		local counter = 0	
		local nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.detailMsBudget)
	
		for instance,record in self.movingRecords do
			self:ProcessDetailObject(record, cameraPos)

			--Cap at 2ms per frame
			counter+=1
			if (counter > 100) then
				counter = 0
				if (tick() > nextPause) then

					debug.profileend()
					task.wait()
					debug.profilebegin("Update Moving Details")
					nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.detailMsBudget) 
				end
			end
		end
	end)
end

function module:Update(dt)
	debug.profilebegin("Update Detail Module")
	self:Setup()

	local startTime = tick()

	for key,value in self.debugTris do
		value:Destroy()
	end
	self.debugTris = {}
	
	local cameraPos = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position
	
	local cameraMoveDist = (cameraPos - self.cameraPreviousCFrame.Position).Magnitude
	self.cameraPreviousCFrame = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame
	
	if (cameraMoveDist > module.teleportSize) then
		--Camera teleported
		if (self.debugging == true) then
			print("Camera teleported!")
		end
		self.detailsDirty = true
		self.supressAnimationFrames += 1
	end
	
	--see if the camera has moved sufficiently far since the last check
	if (self.gridPreviousPos == nil) then
		self.gridPreviousPos = cameraPos 
	end
	local movedSinceDirty = cameraPos - self.gridPreviousPos
	
	if (self.detailsDirty == false) then	
		if (movedSinceDirty.Magnitude > self.stepSize) then
			self.gridPreviousPos = cameraPos 
			self.detailsDirty = true	
		end
	end
	
	self.lastCameraPos = cameraPos;
	
	--Call the various systems
	self:UpdateNewlyVisibleDetails(cameraPos)
	self:UpdateDetails(cameraPos, dt)
	self:UpdateMovingDetails(cameraPos, dt)
	self:UpdateImposters()
	self:UpdateAnimations(dt)
	
	
	if (self.processing == false) then
		if (self.supressAnimationFrames > 0) then
			self.supressAnimationFrames -= 1
		end
	end
	
	local totalTime = math.floor( (tick() - startTime) * 10000)
	self:DrawDebugText(totalTime)

	debug.profileend()
end

function module:UpdateNewlyVisibleDetails(cameraPos)
	--Records that have been snapped into place
	for instance, record in self.newlyVisibleRecords do
		--Clear off any existing animations
		self:ClearAnimations(record)

		--calculate the initial value
		local dist = (self:GetPosition(record) - cameraPos).magnitude
		if (dist > record.distance) then
			
			if (record.reparent == true) then
				record.instance.Parent = nil
			else
				--Set Transparency To full
				self:SnapRecordToTransparent(record)
			end
			
			--Lods
			if (record.lodModel~=nil) then
				record.lodModel.Parent = record.parent
			end
			record.visible = false
		else
			record.visible = true
			record.instance.Parent = record.parent
			
			--Lods
			if (record.lodModel~=nil) then
				record.lodModel.Parent = nil
			end
		end
	end
	self.newlyVisibleRecords = {}
end

function module:DrawDebugText(totalTime)
	debug.profilebegin("DrawDebugText")
	--Debugging text
	if (self.drawDebugText == true) then
		--get it in a format like 3.3ms
	
		totalTime/=10
		local totalTimeString = tostring(totalTime)
		if (totalTime < 0.1) then
			totalTimeString = "0.0"
		end

		if (self.debugGui == nil) then
			local debugGui = Instance.new("ScreenGui")
			debugGui.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui
			debugGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
			debugGui.IgnoreGuiInset = true
			debugGui.Name = "DebugGui"
			self.debugGui = debugGui
		end

		local totalImposters = 0
		self.visibleImposterQuads = 0
		self.visibleImposterModels = 0
		for key,value in self.imposters do
			totalImposters+=1
			if (value.showModel == false) then
				self.visibleImposterQuads += 1
			else
				self.visibleImposterModels += 1
			end
		end
		
		local start = 76
		local y = start
		local step = 14
		self:DrawUIText(Vector3.new(10,y,0), "Num Details: (".. (self.visibleDetails + self.visibleMovingDetails) .. "/" .. self.recordCount ..")", Color3.new(0,1,0), 8)
		y+=step
		self:DrawUIText(Vector3.new(10,y,0), "Animating: "..self.detailsAnimating, Color3.new(0,1,0), 8)
		y+=step
		self:DrawUIText(Vector3.new(10,y,0), "Imposter Models vs Quads: ("..self.visibleImposterModels .. " vs " .. self.visibleImposterQuads ..")", Color3.new(0,1,0), 8)
		y+=step
		self:DrawUIText(Vector3.new(10,y,0), "Imposter Updates: "..self.imposterUpdates, Color3.new(0,1,0), 8)
		y+=step

		self:DrawUIText(Vector3.new(10,y,0), "Detail CPU: "..totalTimeString .. "ms.", Color3.new(0,1,0), 8)
		y+=step

	end
	self.imposterUpdates = 0
	debug.profileend()
end

function module:UpdateImposters()
	if (self.impostersUpdating ~= true) then
		self.impostersUpdating = true
		coroutine.wrap(function()
		 
			--2ms max
			local nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.imposterMsBudget)
			
			--Update imposters
			local counter = 0
			for key,record in self.imposters do
				
				--every 100 updates, see if we need to wait
				counter+=1
				if (counter > 100) then
					if (tick() > nextPause) then
						nextPause = tick() + ((1/1000) * self.imposterMsBudget)
						counter = 0
					 
						task.wait()
					end
				end
				self:UpdateImposter(record)
			end
			self.impostersUpdating = false
			 
		end)()
	end
end		

function module:ImposterSetup(imposterModel)
	if (self.imposters[imposterModel]~=nil) then
		return
	end
	
	local record = {}
	record.instance = imposterModel
	
	record.parent = imposterModel.Parent
	
	record.animate = true
	local animateValue = imposterModel:GetAttribute("animate")
	if (animateValue ~= nil) then
		record.animate = animateValue
	end
 
	record.showModel = true
	
	module.imposters[imposterModel] = record
end

local function CompareAngle(a,b)
	if (math.abs(a-b)>0.5) then
		return true
	end
	return false
end

local function CompareInt(a,b)
	if (math.abs(a-b)>0) then
		return true
	end
	return false
end

local function CompareVector(a,b)
	if (math.abs(a.x-b.x) > 0.1 or math.abs(a.y-b.y) > 0.1 or math.abs(a.z-b.z) > 0.1) then
		return true
	end
	return false
end

local function CompareRotation(a,b)
	return CompareVector(a.LookVector, b.LookVector)
end

function module:UpdateImposterSize(record)
		
	local cf, size = record.instance:GetBoundingBox() 	
	 
	local largest = math.max(math.max(size.x, size.y), size.z) 
	
	largest *= record.scale
		
	--Todo: calculate this based on angle
	for key,part in record.parts do
		local clone = record.surface:Clone()
		clone.Parent = part
		part.Size = Vector3.new(0.00001, largest, largest)
		part.Position = cf.Position
		part.Parent = record.lodModel
		part.Transparency = 1
	end
	
	record.offset = cf.Position - record.instance:GetModelCFrame().Position
	
	record.storedBounds = size
	record.storedCF = cf
	record.storedPivotCF = record.instance:GetModelCFrame()
 
	record.largest = largest
	
	return cf, size
end
 
function module:UpdateImposter(record)
	if (record.surface == nil) then
		
		--Make sure we're streamed in
		if (#record.instance:GetChildren() == 0) then
			return
		end		

		--wait til everything is loaded
		local hasImposter = record.instance:GetAttribute("HasImposter")
		if (hasImposter ~= nil and hasImposter == true) then
			--If we're tagged as having an imposter, we have to wait for it to be replicated			
			if record.instance:FindFirstChild("Imposter", true) == nil then
				return
			end
		end
	 
		local model = record.instance:FindFirstChild("Imposter", true)
		if (model == nil) then
			--Try the replicatedFirst/Imposter folder
			if (self.folder == nil) then
				return
			end
			model = self.folder:FindFirstChild(record.instance.Name)
			if (model) then
				model = model:Clone()
				model.Parent = record.instance
			else
				return				
			end
		end

		record.surface = model:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("SurfaceAppearance")
		if (record.surface ~= nil) then
  		
			--Gather parts
			record.parts = {}
			for j=1,16 do
				local part = module.quads:FindFirstChild("Quad"..j):Clone()
				record.parts[j] = part
				part.Position = record.instance:GetModelCFrame().Position
				--v1.1 - shadow casting is copied 
				part.CastShadow = model.CastShadow
			end
			
			--grab any attributes off it
			record.scale = 1
			local newScale = model:GetAttribute("scale")
			if (newScale ~= nil and tonumber(newScale) ~= nil and newScale > 0) then
				record.scale = newScale
			end
			
			--Remove this so it doesnt count for bounds
			model:Destroy()
			
			--Create a model to hold the billboards
			local imposterModel = Instance.new("Model")
			imposterModel.Name = record.instance.Name .. "_Imp"
			imposterModel.Parent = record.parent
			
			record.lodModel = imposterModel
						
			record.instance.DescendantAdded:Connect(function()
				--recalculate the bounds if a child is added after now (we need the real size, but dont want to calculate it every frame)
				if (record.storedBounds ~= nil) then
					local cf, size = record.instance:GetBoundingBox()
					local mag = record.storedBounds - size
					if (mag.magnitude > 0) then
						record.storedBounds = nil
					end
				end
				--record.storedBounds = nil
			end)
						
			record.baseRotation = CFrame.fromEulerAngles(math.rad(90),0,0)
			record.ang = 0
		end
	end
	
	if (record.surface == nil) then
		return
	end
	
	if (record.storedBounds == nil) then
		self:UpdateImposterSize(record)
	end	
	
	local parentPivot = record.storedCF

	--Get the angle of the billboard 
	local modelPosition = parentPivot.Position
	
	local vec = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position - modelPosition
	
	local prevShowModel = record.showModel
 
	record.showModel = false
 
	local mag = vec.Magnitude
	if (self.debugSupression == true) then
		mag = 0
	end
	
	--Deparent if we're beyond the imposterMaxDistance
	if (mag > module.imposterMaxDistance) then
		if (record.lodModel.Parent ~= nil) then
			record.lodModel.Parent = nil
		end
	else
		if (record.lodModel.Parent == nil) then
			record.lodModel.Parent = record.instance.Parent	
		end
	end	
	 			
	if (mag < module.imposterDistance) then
		record.showModel = true
	end

	
	if (record.showModel == false) then
		--check for verticality
		local angle = math.abs(vec.Unit.y)
		if (angle > self.imposterVerticalAngleTolerance) then
			record.showModel = true
		end
	end
	
	
	if (record.showModel ~= prevShowModel ) then
		if (record.showModel == false) then
			self:AnimateRecord(record, 1 * self.imposterAnimSpeed) --Fade out
		end
		if (record.showModel == true) then
			record.instance.Parent = record.parent
			self:AnimateRecord(record, -1 * self.imposterAnimSpeed) --Fade in
		end
	end
	
	--Showing the imposter	
	if (record.showModel == false) then
	 
		local flatVec = Vector3.new(vec.x, 0, vec.z)
		local unit = flatVec.Unit
		local angle = math.atan2(-unit.z, unit.x)

		--Get the angle of the tree 
		local steps = 360 / (16)

		local startingVec = record.storedPivotCF.RightVector
		local startFlatVec = Vector3.new(startingVec.x, 0, startingVec.z).Unit
		local startingAngle = -math.atan2(-startFlatVec.z, startFlatVec.x)
		
		--local frameAngle = math.deg(angle) + math.deg(startingAngle) + 90
		local frameAngle = math.deg(angle) + math.deg(startingAngle) + 90
		
		--   -_-'
		while (frameAngle < 0) do
			frameAngle+=360
		end
		while (frameAngle > 360) do
			frameAngle-=360
		end
		local partIndex = math.floor(frameAngle / steps) + 1
		
		if (record.prevPartIndex == nil or 
			CompareInt(record.prevPartIndex, partIndex) == true or
			CompareAngle(record.prevAngle, angle) == true or
			CompareVector(record.prevModelPosition, modelPosition) == true) then
			
		 	self.imposterUpdates+=1
			local partToUse = record.parts[partIndex]

			for i = 1,16 do
				if (i == partIndex) then
					record.parts[i].Transparency = 0
				else
					record.parts[i].Transparency = 1
				end
			end	
			partToUse.CFrame = CFrame.new(modelPosition) * CFrame.fromEulerAngles(0,angle + math.pi,0) * record.baseRotation
		end
				
		--Latches
		record.prevPartIndex = partIndex
		record.prevAngle = angle
		record.prevModelPosition = modelPosition
		record.prevBaseRotation = record.baseRotation
	end
end


function module:Start()
	local userInput = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	
	if (self.allowDebug) then
		userInput.InputBegan:Connect(function(inputObject)
 
			if (inputObject.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard) then
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F8) then
					self.drawDebugText = not self.drawDebugText
				end
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F7) then
					
					self.debugSupression = true
					local pos = game.workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position
					for instance,record in self.records do
						self:UpdateVis(record, pos)		
					end
				end
			end
		end)

		userInput.InputEnded:Connect(function(inputObject)
			if (inputObject.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard) then
				if (inputObject.KeyCode==Enum.KeyCode.F7) then
					
					self.debugSupression = false
					local pos = game.workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position
					for instance,record in self.records do
						self:UpdateVis(record, pos)
					end
				end
			end
		end)
	end
	
	game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(dt)
		module:Update(dt)
	end)
end

module:Start()

return module
